```text
# This file configures the analyzer, which statically analyzes Dart code to
# check for errors, warnings, and lints.
#
# The issues identified by the analyzer are surfaced in the UI of Dart-enabled
# IDEs (https://dart.dev/tools#ides-and-editors). The analyzer can also be
# invoked from the command line by running `flutter analyze`.

# The following line activates a set of recommended lints for Flutter apps,
# packages, and plugins designed to encourage good coding practices.
include: package:flutter_lints/flutter.yaml

linter:
  # The lint rules applied to this project can be customized in the
  # section below to disable rules from the `package:flutter_lints/flutter.yaml`
  # included above or to enable additional rules. A list of all available lints
  # and their documentation is published at https://dart.dev/lints.
  #
  # Instead of disabling a lint rule for the entire project in the
  # section below, it can also be suppressed for a single line of code
  # or a specific dart file by using the `// ignore: name_of_lint` and
  # `// ignore_for_file: name_of_lint` syntax on the line or in the file
```

### File 10: gradlew
**Path:** `android\gradlew`
**Size:** 4.85 KB

```text
#!/usr/bin/env bash

##############################################################################
##
##  Gradle start up script for UN*X
##
##############################################################################

# Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=""

APP_NAME="Gradle"
APP_BASE_NAME=`basename "$0"`

# Use the maximum available, or set MAX_FD != -1 to use that value.
MAX_FD="maximum"

warn ( ) {
    echo "$*"
}

die ( ) {
    echo
    echo "$*"
    echo
    exit 1
}

# OS specific support (must be 'true' or 'false').
cygwin=false
msys=false
darwin=false
case "`uname`" in
  CYGWIN* )
    cygwin=true
    ;;
  Darwin* )
    darwin=true
    ;;
  MINGW* )
    msys=true
    ;;
esac

# Attempt to set APP_HOME
# Resolve links: $0 may be a link
PRG="$0"
# Need this for relative symlinks.
while [ -h "$PRG" ] ; do
    ls=`ls -ld "$PRG"`
    link=`expr "$ls" : '.*-> \(.*\)$'`
    if expr "$link" : '/.*' > /dev/null; then
        PRG="$link"
    else
        PRG=`dirname "$PRG"`"/$link"
    fi
done
SAVED="`pwd`"
cd "`dirname \"$PRG\"`/" >/dev/null
APP_HOME="`pwd -P`"
cd "$SAVED" >/dev/null

CLASSPATH=$APP_HOME/gradle/wrapper/gradle-wrapper.jar

# Determine the Java command to use to start the JVM.
if [ -n "$JAVA_HOME" ] ; then
    if [ -x "$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java" ] ; then
        # IBM's JDK on AIX uses strange locations for the executables
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java"
    else
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/bin/java"
    fi
    if [ ! -x "$JAVACMD" ] ; then
        die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: $JAVA_HOME

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
    fi
else
    JAVACMD="java"
    which java >/dev/null 2>&1 || die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
fi

# Increase the maximum file descriptors if we can.
if [ "$cygwin" = "false" -a "$darwin" = "false" ] ; then
    MAX_FD_LIMIT=`ulimit -H -n`
    if [ $? -eq 0 ] ; then
        if [ "$MAX_FD" = "maximum" -o "$MAX_FD" = "max" ] ; then
            MAX_FD="$MAX_FD_LIMIT"
        fi
        ulimit -n $MAX_FD
        if [ $? -ne 0 ] ; then
            warn "Could not set maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD"
        fi
    else
        warn "Could not query maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD_LIMIT"
    fi
fi

# For Darwin, add options to specify how the application appears in the dock
if $darwin; then
    GRADLE_OPTS="$GRADLE_OPTS \"-Xdock:name=$APP_NAME\" \"-Xdock:icon=$APP_HOME/media/gradle.icns\""
fi

# For Cygwin, switch paths to Windows format before running java
if $cygwin ; then
    APP_HOME=`cygpath --path --mixed "$APP_HOME"`
    CLASSPATH=`cygpath --path --mixed "$CLASSPATH"`
    JAVACMD=`cygpath --unix "$JAVACMD"`

    # We build the pattern for arguments to be converted via cygpath
    ROOTDIRSRAW=`find -L / -maxdepth 1 -mindepth 1 -type d 2>/dev/null`
    SEP=""
    for dir in $ROOTDIRSRAW ; do
        ROOTDIRS="$ROOTDIRS$SEP$dir"
        SEP="|"
    done
    OURCYGPATTERN="(^($ROOTDIRS))"
    # Add a user-defined pattern to the cygpath arguments
    if [ "$GRADLE_CYGPATTERN" != "" ] ; then
        OURCYGPATTERN="$OURCYGPATTERN|($GRADLE_CYGPATTERN)"
    fi
    # Now convert the arguments - kludge to limit ourselves to /bin/sh
    i=0
    for arg in "$@" ; do
        CHECK=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "$OURCYGPATTERN" -`
        CHECK2=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "^-"`                                 ### Determine if an option

        if [ $CHECK -ne 0 ] && [ $CHECK2 -eq 0 ] ; then                    ### Added a condition
            eval `echo args$i`=`cygpath --path --ignore --mixed "$arg"`
        else
            eval `echo args$i`="\"$arg\""
        fi
        i=$((i+1))
    done
    case $i in
        (0) set -- ;;
        (1) set -- "$args0" ;;
        (2) set -- "$args0" "$args1" ;;
        (3) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" ;;
        (4) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" ;;
        (5) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" ;;
        (6) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" ;;
        (7) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" ;;
        (8) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" ;;
        (9) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" "$args8" ;;
    esac
fi

# Split up the JVM_OPTS And GRADLE_OPTS values into an array, following the shell quoting and substitution rules
function splitJvmOpts() {
    JVM_OPTS=("$@")
}
eval splitJvmOpts $DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS $JAVA_OPTS $GRADLE_OPTS
JVM_OPTS[${#JVM_OPTS[*]}]="-Dorg.gradle.appname=$APP_BASE_NAME"

exec "$JAVACMD" "${JVM_OPTS[@]}" -classpath "$CLASSPATH" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain "$@"

```

### File 11: gradlew.bat
**Path:** `android\gradlew.bat`
**Size:** 2.35 KB

```text
@if "%DEBUG%" == "" @echo off
@rem ##########################################################################
@rem
@rem  Gradle startup script for Windows
@rem
@rem ##########################################################################

@rem Set local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" setlocal

@rem Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
set DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=

set DIRNAME=%~dp0
if "%DIRNAME%" == "" set DIRNAME=.
set APP_BASE_NAME=%~n0
set APP_HOME=%DIRNAME%

@rem Find java.exe
if defined JAVA_HOME goto findJavaFromJavaHome

set JAVA_EXE=java.exe
%JAVA_EXE% -version >NUL 2>&1
if "%ERRORLEVEL%" == "0" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:findJavaFromJavaHome
set JAVA_HOME=%JAVA_HOME:"=%
set JAVA_EXE=%JAVA_HOME%/bin/java.exe

if exist "%JAVA_EXE%" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: %JAVA_HOME%
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:init
@rem Get command-line arguments, handling Windowz variants

if not "%OS%" == "Windows_NT" goto win9xME_args
if "%@eval[2+2]" == "4" goto 4NT_args

:win9xME_args
@rem Slurp the command line arguments.
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=
set _SKIP=2

:win9xME_args_slurp
if "x%~1" == "x" goto execute

set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%*
goto execute

:4NT_args
@rem Get arguments from the 4NT Shell from JP Software
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%$

:execute
@rem Setup the command line

set CLASSPATH=%APP_HOME%\gradle\wrapper\gradle-wrapper.jar

@rem Execute Gradle
"%JAVA_EXE%" %DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS% %JAVA_OPTS% %GRADLE_OPTS% "-Dorg.gradle.appname=%APP_BASE_NAME%" -classpath "%CLASSPATH%" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain %CMD_LINE_ARGS%

:end
@rem End local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%ERRORLEVEL%"=="0" goto mainEnd

:fail
rem Set variable GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE if you need the _script_ return code instead of
rem the _cmd.exe /c_ return code!
if  not "" == "%GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE%" exit 1
exit /b 1

:mainEnd
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" endlocal

:omega

```

```gradle
pluginManagement {
    def flutterSdkPath = {
        def properties = new Properties()
        file("local.properties").withInputStream { properties.load(it) }
        def flutterSdkPath = properties.getProperty("flutter.sdk")
        assert flutterSdkPath != null, "flutter.sdk not set in local.properties"
        return flutterSdkPath
    }()

    includeBuild("$flutterSdkPath/packages/flutter_tools/gradle")

    repositories {
        google()

        gradlePluginPortal()
```

```dart
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {

      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
      theme: ThemeData(
        useMaterial3: true,
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class OnboardingItem {
  final String title;
  final String description;
  final IconData primaryIcon;
  final IconData secondaryIcon;
  final Color accentColor;

  const OnboardingItem({
    required this.title,
    required this.description,
    required this.primaryIcon,
    required this.secondaryIcon,
    required this.accentColor,
  });
}

class OnboardingData {
  // âœ… CORRECT ORDER - As per your screenshots
  static const List<OnboardingItem> items = [
    // Screen 1: Store All Documents (Cyan)
    OnboardingItem(
      title: 'Store All Documents',
      description: 'Aadhaar, PAN, certificates safely\nin your digital vault',
      primaryIcon: Icons.verified_user,
      secondaryIcon: Icons.description,
      accentColor: Color(0xFF00BCD4), // Cyan
    ),

    // Screen 2: Secure Your Vault (Blue)
    OnboardingItem(
      title: 'Secure Your Vault',
      description: 'Protect your data with PIN/\nbiometric authentication',
      primaryIcon: Icons.fingerprint,
      secondaryIcon: Icons.lock,
      accentColor: Color(0xFF2196F3), // Blue
    ),

    // Screen 3: Identity Documents (Green)
    OnboardingItem(
      title: 'Identity Documents',
      description: 'Quick access to all your identity\ndocuments in one place',
      primaryIcon: Icons.badge,
      secondaryIcon: Icons.star,
      accentColor: Color(0xFF4CAF50), // Green
    ),
  ];

  static int get itemCount => items.length;

  static OnboardingItem getItem(int index) {
    if (index >= 0 && index < items.length) {
      return items[index];
    }
    return items[0];
  }

  static bool isLastPage(int currentPage) {
    return currentPage == items.length - 1;
  }

  static bool isFirstPage(int currentPage) {
    return currentPage == 0;
  }

  static String getButtonText(int currentPage) {
    return isLastPage(currentPage) ? 'Get Started' : 'Next';
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class DocumentCategory {
  final String id;
  final String name;
  final String subtitle;
  final IconData icon;
  final int documentCount;

  const DocumentCategory({
    required this.id,
    required this.name,
    required this.subtitle,
    required this.icon,
    this.documentCount = 0,
  });

  DocumentCategory copyWith({int? documentCount}) {
    return DocumentCategory(
      id: id,
      name: name,
      subtitle: subtitle,
      icon: icon,
      documentCount: documentCount ?? this.documentCount,
    );
  }
}
```

### File 40: document_item.dart
**Path:** `lib\core\models\document_item.dart`
**Size:** 2.12 KB

```dart
class DocumentItem {
  final String id;
  final String name;
  final String categoryId;
  final DateTime addedAt;
  final String? thumbnailPath;
  final int fileSize;
  final String fileType;
  final bool isEncrypted; // ğŸ†• NEW

  const DocumentItem({
    required this.id,
    required this.name,
    required this.categoryId,
    required this.addedAt,
    this.thumbnailPath,
    required this.fileSize,
    required this.fileType,
    this.isEncrypted = false, // ğŸ†• NEW
  });

  Map<String, dynamic> toJson() {
    return {
      'id': id,
      'name': name,
      'categoryId': categoryId,
      'addedAt': addedAt.toIso8601String(),
      'thumbnailPath': thumbnailPath,
      'fileSize': fileSize,
      'fileType': fileType,
      'isEncrypted': isEncrypted, // ğŸ†• NEW
    };
  }

  factory DocumentItem.fromJson(Map<String, dynamic> json) {
    return DocumentItem(
      id: json['id'] as String,
      name: json['name'] as String,
      categoryId: json['categoryId'] as String,
      addedAt: DateTime.parse(json['addedAt'] as String),
      thumbnailPath: json['thumbnailPath'] as String?,
      fileSize: json['fileSize'] as int,
      fileType: json['fileType'] as String? ?? 'image',
      isEncrypted: json['isEncrypted'] as bool? ?? false, // ğŸ†• NEW
    );
  }

  bool get isPdf => fileType == 'pdf';
  bool get isImage => fileType == 'image';
  bool get hasEncryption => isEncrypted; // ğŸ†• NEW

  String getTimeAgo() {
    final now = DateTime.now();
    final difference = now.difference(addedAt);
    if (difference.inDays > 0) {
      return '${difference.inDays} day${difference.inDays > 1 ? 's' : ''} ago';
    } else if (difference.inHours > 0) {
      return '${difference.inHours} hour${difference.inHours > 1 ? 's' : ''} ago';
    } else {
      return 'Just now';
    }
  }

  String getFileSizeFormatted() {
    if (fileSize < 1024) {
      return '$fileSize B';
    } else if (fileSize < 1024 * 1024) {
      return '${(fileSize / 1024).toStringAsFixed(1)} KB';
    } else {
      return '${(fileSize / (1024 * 1024)).toStringAsFixed(1)} MB';
    }
  }
}

```

### File 42: app_initialization_service.dart
**Path:** `lib\core\services\app_initialization_service.dart`
**Size:** 3.02 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter_secure_storage/flutter_secure_storage.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';

/// App initialization service - Decides which screen to show on app start
class AppInitializationService {
  // âœ… Storage Keys
  static const String _onboardingCompletedKey = 'is_onboarding_completed';
  static const String _pinSetKey = 'is_pin_set';
  static const String _userPinKey = 'user_pin';

  final FlutterSecureStorage _secureStorage = const FlutterSecureStorage();

  /// âœ… Determine the initial route based on app state
  Future<String> determineInitialRoute() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();

      // STEP 1: Check if onboarding is completed
      final isOnboardingCompleted = prefs.getBool(_onboardingCompletedKey) ?? false;
      if (!isOnboardingCompleted) {
        return '/onboarding';
      }

      // STEP 2: Check if PIN is set
      final isPinSet = prefs.getBool(_pinSetKey) ?? false;
      if (!isPinSet) {
        return '/createpin';  // âœ… First time â†’ Setup Mode
      }

      // STEP 3: Verify PIN exists in secure storage
      final savedPin = await _secureStorage.read(key: _userPinKey);
      if (savedPin == null || savedPin.isEmpty) {
        // Data corruption - reset PIN flag and force PIN creation
        await prefs.setBool(_pinSetKey, false);
        return '/createpin';
      }

      // STEP 4: All checks passed - go to PIN entry screen
      return '/enterpin';  // âœ… Next times â†’ Verify Mode

    } catch (e) {
      // On any error, safe fallback to onboarding
      return '/onboarding';
    }
  }

  /// âœ… Mark onboarding as completed
  Future<bool> setOnboardingCompleted() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      return await prefs.setBool(_onboardingCompletedKey, true);
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// Check if onboarding is completed
  Future<bool> isOnboardingCompleted() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      return prefs.getBool(_onboardingCompletedKey) ?? false;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// âœ… Mark PIN as set
  Future<bool> setPinCompleted() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      return await prefs.setBool(_pinSetKey, true);
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// Check if PIN is set
  Future<bool> isPinSet() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      return prefs.getBool(_pinSetKey) ?? false;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// âœ… Reset all app state (for testing or logout)
  Future<void> resetAppState() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      await prefs.remove(_onboardingCompletedKey);
      await prefs.remove(_pinSetKey);
      await _secureStorage.delete(key: _userPinKey);
    } catch (e) {
      // Silent fail
    }
  }
}
```

### File 43: app_lifecycle_service.dart
**Path:** `lib\core\services\app_lifecycle_service.dart`
**Size:** 4.49 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import 'secure_storage_service.dart';

class AppLifecycleService with WidgetsBindingObserver {
  static final AppLifecycleService _instance = AppLifecycleService._internal();
  factory AppLifecycleService() => _instance;
  AppLifecycleService._internal();

  static AppLifecycleService get instance => _instance;

  final secureStorage = SecureStorageServiceFactory.create();

  static const String _authStatusKey = 'is_authenticated';
  static const String _lastActiveKey = 'last_active_timestamp';
  static const String _backgroundTimeKey = 'background_timestamp';

  static const int autoLockMinutes = 5;
  static const int backgroundLockSeconds = 30;

  AppLifecycleState? _lastLifecycleState;
  bool _isInitialized = false;

  static void initialize() {
    _instance._init();
  }

  void _init() {
    if (!_isInitialized) {
      WidgetsBinding.instance.addObserver(this);
      _isInitialized = true;
      debugPrint('âœ… AppLifecycleService: Initialized');
    }
  }

  void dispose() {
    if (_isInitialized) {
      WidgetsBinding.instance.removeObserver(this);
      _isInitialized = false;
      debugPrint('ğŸ”´ AppLifecycleService: Disposed');
    }
  }

  @override
  void didChangeAppLifecycleState(AppLifecycleState state) {
    debugPrint('ğŸ”„ AppLifecycleService: Lifecycle changed to $state');

    if (_isGoingToBackground(state)) {
      _handleAppPaused();
    }

    if (_isReturningToForeground(state)) {
      _handleAppResumed();
    }

    _lastLifecycleState = state;
  }

  bool _isGoingToBackground(AppLifecycleState state) {
    return state == AppLifecycleState.paused ||
        state == AppLifecycleState.inactive ||
        state == AppLifecycleState.hidden;
  }

  bool _isReturningToForeground(AppLifecycleState state) {
    return (_lastLifecycleState == AppLifecycleState.paused ||
        _lastLifecycleState == AppLifecycleState.inactive ||
        _lastLifecycleState == AppLifecycleState.hidden) &&
        state == AppLifecycleState.resumed;
  }

  Future<void> _handleAppPaused() async {
    debugPrint('â¸ï¸ AppLifecycleService: App paused');
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.setString(_backgroundTimeKey, DateTime.now().toIso8601String());
  }

  Future<void> _handleAppResumed() async {
    debugPrint('â–¶ï¸ AppLifecycleService: App resumed');
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final backgroundTimeStr = prefs.getString(_backgroundTimeKey);

    if (backgroundTimeStr != null) {
      final backgroundTime = DateTime.parse(backgroundTimeStr);
      final now = DateTime.now();
      final secondsInBackground = now.difference(backgroundTime).inSeconds;

      if (secondsInBackground >= backgroundLockSeconds) {
        debugPrint(
            'ğŸ”’ AppLifecycleService: Auto-locking (background > $backgroundLockSeconds seconds)');
        await logout();
      }
    }
  }

  Future<void> authenticateUser() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.setBool(_authStatusKey, true);
    await prefs.setString(_lastActiveKey, DateTime.now().toIso8601String());
    debugPrint('âœ… AppLifecycleService: User authenticated');
  }

  Future<bool> isAuthenticated() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final isAuth = prefs.getBool(_authStatusKey) ?? false;

    if (!isAuth) return false;

    final lastActiveStr = prefs.getString(_lastActiveKey);
    if (lastActiveStr == null) return false;

    final lastActive = DateTime.parse(lastActiveStr);
    final now = DateTime.now();
    final minutesInactive = now.difference(lastActive).inMinutes;

    if (minutesInactive >= autoLockMinutes) {
      debugPrint('â±ï¸ AppLifecycleService: Session expired');
      await logout();
      return false;
    }

    await prefs.setString(_lastActiveKey, now.toIso8601String());
    return true;
  }

  Future<void> logout() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.setBool(_authStatusKey, false);
    await prefs.remove(_lastActiveKey);
    await prefs.remove(_backgroundTimeKey);
    debugPrint('ğŸšª AppLifecycleService: User logged out');
  }

  Future<void> updateLastActive() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.setString(_lastActiveKey, DateTime.now().toIso8601String());
  }
}
```

### File 44: auth_service.dart

```dart
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';

class AuthService {
  static final AuthService _instance = AuthService._internal();
  factory AuthService() => _instance;
  AuthService._internal();

  static const String _pinKey = 'user_pin';
  static const String _isLockedKey = 'is_locked';
  static const String _lastActiveKey = 'last_active_time';
  static const int autoLockMinutes = 5;

  Future<bool> setPin(String pin) async {
    try {
      if (!_isValidPin(pin)) {
        debugPrint('AuthService: Invalid PIN format');
        return false;
      }

      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final success = await prefs.setString(_pinKey, pin);

      if (success) {
        await _setLockState(false);
        await _updateLastActiveTime();
        debugPrint('AuthService: PIN saved successfully');
      }

      return success;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error saving PIN - ${e.toString()}');
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<bool> verifyPin(String enteredPin) async {
    try {
      if (!_isValidPin(enteredPin)) {
        debugPrint('AuthService: Invalid PIN format');
        return false;
      }

      final savedPin = await _getSavedPin();

      if (savedPin == null) {
        debugPrint('AuthService: No PIN set');
        return false;
      }

      final isCorrect = savedPin == enteredPin;

      if (isCorrect) {
        await _setLockState(false);
        await _updateLastActiveTime();
        debugPrint('AuthService: PIN verified successfully');
      } else {
        debugPrint('AuthService: Incorrect PIN');
      }

      return isCorrect;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error verifying PIN - ${e.toString()}');
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<bool> isPinSet() async {
    try {
      final pin = await _getSavedPin();
      return pin != null && pin.isNotEmpty;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error checking PIN status - ${e.toString()}');
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<bool> isLocked() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final locked = prefs.getBool(_isLockedKey) ?? true;

      if (!locked) {
        final shouldAutoLock = await _shouldAutoLock();
        if (shouldAutoLock) {
          await lock();
          return true;
        }
      }

      return locked;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error checking lock status - ${e.toString()}');
      return true;
    }
  }

  Future<void> lock() async {
    try {
      await _setLockState(true);
      debugPrint('AuthService: App locked');
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error locking app - ${e.toString()}');
    }
  }

  Future<void> unlock() async {
    try {
      await _setLockState(false);
      await _updateLastActiveTime();
      debugPrint('AuthService: App unlocked');
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error unlocking app - ${e.toString()}');
    }
  }

  Future<void> updateActivity() async {
    try {
      final locked = await isLocked();
      if (!locked) {
        await _updateLastActiveTime();
      }
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error updating activity - ${e.toString()}');
    }
  }

  Future<bool> resetPin() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      await prefs.remove(_pinKey);
      await prefs.remove(_isLockedKey);
      await prefs.remove(_lastActiveKey);
      debugPrint('AuthService: PIN reset successfully');
      return true;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error resetting PIN - ${e.toString()}');
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<bool> changePin(String oldPin, String newPin) async {
    try {
      final isOldPinCorrect = await verifyPin(oldPin);
      if (!isOldPinCorrect) {
        debugPrint('AuthService: Old PIN verification failed');
        return false;
      }

      return await setPin(newPin);
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error changing PIN - ${e.toString()}');
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<String?> _getSavedPin() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      return prefs.getString(_pinKey);
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error getting saved PIN - ${e.toString()}');
      return null;
    }
  }

  Future<void> _setLockState(bool locked) async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      await prefs.setBool(_isLockedKey, locked);
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error setting lock state - ${e.toString()}');
    }
  }

  Future<void> _updateLastActiveTime() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final timestamp = DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
      await prefs.setInt(_lastActiveKey, timestamp);
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error updating last active time - ${e.toString()}');
    }
  }

  Future<bool> _shouldAutoLock() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final lastActiveTimestamp = prefs.getInt(_lastActiveKey);

      if (lastActiveTimestamp == null) {
        return true;
      }

      final lastActiveTime = DateTime.fromMillisecondsSinceEpoch(lastActiveTimestamp);
      final now = DateTime.now();
      final difference = now.difference(lastActiveTime);

      return difference.inMinutes >= autoLockMinutes;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('AuthService: Error checking auto-lock - ${e.toString()}');
      return true;
    }
  }

  bool _isValidPin(String pin) {
    if (pin.length != 4) {
      return false;
    }

    return RegExp(r'^\d{4}$').hasMatch(pin);
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:local_auth/local_auth.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
import 'dart:io' show Platform;
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart' show kIsWeb;

class BiometricService {
  static final BiometricService _instance = BiometricService._internal();
  factory BiometricService() => _instance;
  BiometricService._internal();

  final LocalAuthentication _localAuth = LocalAuthentication();

  /// âœ… FIXED: Platform-aware biometric availability check
  Future<bool> isDeviceSupported() async {
    try {
      // âœ… WINDOWS BYPASS: Always return true on Windows for development
      if (!kIsWeb && Platform.isWindows) {
        return true; // Enable biometric UI on Windows (will simulate)
      }

      return await _localAuth.isDeviceSupported();
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// âœ… FIXED: Check biometric availability with Windows support
  Future<bool> isBiometricAvailable() async {
    try {
      // âœ… WINDOWS BYPASS: Always return true for UI display
      if (!kIsWeb && Platform.isWindows) {
        return true; // Show biometric button on Windows
      }

      final isSupported = await _localAuth.isDeviceSupported();
      if (!isSupported) return false;

      final availableBiometrics = await _localAuth.getAvailableBiometrics();
      return availableBiometrics.isNotEmpty;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// âœ… Get available biometrics (with Windows handling)
  Future<List<BiometricType>> getAvailableBiometrics() async {
    try {
      // âœ… WINDOWS SIMULATION: Return fingerprint as available
      if (!kIsWeb && Platform.isWindows) {
        return [BiometricType.fingerprint]; // Simulate fingerprint sensor
      }

      return await _localAuth.getAvailableBiometrics();
    } catch (e) {
      return [];
    }
  }

  /// âœ… FIXED: Authenticate with Windows simulation
  Future<BiometricAuthResult> authenticate() async {
    try {
      // âœ… WINDOWS SIMULATION: Auto-approve authentication
      if (!kIsWeb && Platform.isWindows) {
        // Simulate authentication delay
        await Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 1));

        // Return success (simulated)
        return BiometricAuthResult(
          success: true,
          error: null,
        );
      }

      final isAvailable = await isBiometricAvailable();
      if (!isAvailable) {
        return BiometricAuthResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Biometric not available',
        );
      }

      final authenticated = await _localAuth.authenticate(
        localizedReason: 'Please authenticate to access your documents',
        options: const AuthenticationOptions(
          stickyAuth: true,
          biometricOnly: true,
          useErrorDialogs: true,
        ),
      );

      return BiometricAuthResult(
        success: authenticated,
        error: authenticated ? null : 'Authentication failed',
      );
    } on PlatformException catch (e) {
      String errorMessage = 'Authentication error';

      switch (e.code) {
        case 'NotAvailable':
          errorMessage = 'Biometric authentication not available';
          break;
        case 'NotEnrolled':
          errorMessage = 'No biometric enrolled';
          break;
        case 'LockedOut':
          errorMessage = 'Too many attempts. Try again later';
          break;
        case 'PermanentlyLockedOut':
          errorMessage = 'Biometric authentication disabled';
          break;
        default:
          errorMessage = e.message ?? 'Authentication failed';
      }

      return BiometricAuthResult(
        success: false,
        error: errorMessage,
      );
    } catch (e) {
      return BiometricAuthResult(
        success: false,
        error: 'Unexpected error occurred',
      );
    }
  }

  /// Get biometric type name
  String getBiometricTypeName(BiometricType type) {
    switch (type) {
      case BiometricType.face:
        return 'Face Recognition';
      case BiometricType.fingerprint:
        return 'Fingerprint';
      case BiometricType.iris:
        return 'Iris Scan';
      case BiometricType.strong:
        return 'Strong Biometric';
      case BiometricType.weak:
        return 'Weak Biometric';
      default:
        return 'Biometric';
    }
  }
}

/// Result class for biometric authentication
class BiometricAuthResult {
  final bool success;
  final String? error;

  BiometricAuthResult({
    required this.success,
    this.error,
  });
}
```

```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:image_picker/image_picker.dart';
import 'package:permission_handler/permission_handler.dart';

class CameraService {
  static final CameraService _instance = CameraService._internal();
  factory CameraService() => _instance;
  CameraService._internal();

  final ImagePicker _picker = ImagePicker();

  /// 1ï¸âƒ£ Camera permission check + request
  Future<bool> requestCameraPermission() async {
    final status = await Permission.camera.status;

    if (status.isGranted) {
      return true;
    }

    if (status.isDenied) {
      final result = await Permission.camera.request();
      return result.isGranted;
    }

    // Permanently denied - open settings
    if (status.isPermanentlyDenied) {
      await openAppSettings();
      return false;
    }

    return false;
  }

  /// 2ï¸âƒ£ Check if camera is available
  Future<bool> isCameraAvailable() async {
    try {
      final status = await Permission.camera.status;
      return status.isGranted || status.isDenied;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// 3ï¸âƒ£ Main method: Capture photo from camera
  Future<CameraResult> captureFromCamera() async {
    try {
      // Step 1: Check permission
      final permissionGranted = await requestCameraPermission();
      if (!permissionGranted) {
        return CameraResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Camera permission denied. Please enable it in settings.',
        );
      }

      // Step 2: Open camera and capture
      final XFile? photo = await _picker.pickImage(
        source: ImageSource.camera,
        imageQuality: 85, // Compress to reduce file size
        preferredCameraDevice: CameraDevice.rear,
      );

      // Step 3: Handle cancellation
      if (photo == null) {
        return CameraResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Photo capture cancelled',
        );
      }

      // Step 4: Validate file
      final File imageFile = File(photo.path);
      if (!await imageFile.exists()) {
        return CameraResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Captured file not found',
        );
      }

      final fileSize = await imageFile.length();
      if (fileSize == 0) {
        return CameraResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Captured file is empty',
        );
      }

      // Step 5: Return success with file
      return CameraResult(
        success: true,
        imageFile: imageFile,
        xFile: photo,
      );
    } catch (e) {
      return CameraResult(
        success: false,
        error: 'Failed to capture photo: ${e.toString()}',
      );
    }
  }
}

/// Result model for camera operations
class CameraResult {
  final bool success;
  final File? imageFile;
  final XFile? xFile;
  final String? error;

  CameraResult({
    required this.success,
    this.imageFile,
    this.xFile,
    this.error,
  });
}
```

### File 47: document_storage_service.dart
**Path:** `lib\core\services\document_storage_service.dart`
**Size:** 11.77 KB

```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'dart:convert';
import 'dart:typed_data';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';
import 'package:path/path.dart' as path;
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import 'package:encrypt/encrypt.dart' as encrypt;
import 'package:crypto/crypto.dart';
import '../models/document_item.dart'; // âœ… FIXED - Only 1 dot

class DocumentStorageService {
  static final DocumentStorageService _instance = DocumentStorageService._internal();
  factory DocumentStorageService() => _instance;
  DocumentStorageService._internal();

  static const String _documentsKey = 'saved_documents';

  encrypt.Key? _encryptionKey;
  final _iv = encrypt.IV.fromLength(16);

  Future<void> initializeEncryption(String pin) async {
    try {
      final pinBytes = utf8.encode(pin);
      final hash = sha256.convert(pinBytes);
      _encryptionKey = encrypt.Key(Uint8List.fromList(hash.bytes));
      debugPrint('âœ… Encryption initialized');
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Error: $e');
      rethrow;
    }
  }

  bool get isEncryptionReady => _encryptionKey != null;

  Future<Uint8List> _encryptFileContent(Uint8List fileBytes) async {
    if (_encryptionKey == null) throw Exception('Encryption not initialized');
    try {
      final encrypter = encrypt.Encrypter(encrypt.AES(_encryptionKey!));
      final encrypted = encrypter.encryptBytes(fileBytes, iv: _iv);
      return encrypted.bytes;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Encryption error: $e');
      rethrow;
    }
  }

  Future<Uint8List> _decryptFileContent(Uint8List encryptedBytes) async {
    if (_encryptionKey == null) throw Exception('Encryption not initialized');
    try {
      final encrypter = encrypt.Encrypter(encrypt.AES(_encryptionKey!));
      final encrypted = encrypt.Encrypted(encryptedBytes);
      final decrypted = encrypter.decryptBytes(encrypted, iv: _iv);
      return Uint8List.fromList(decrypted);
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Decryption error: $e');
      rethrow;
    }
  }

  Future<SaveResult> saveDocument({
    required File imageFile,
    required String documentName,
    required String categoryId,
  }) async {
    try {
      final String fileExtension = path.extension(imageFile.path).toLowerCase();
      final String fileType = _detectFileType(fileExtension);

      if (fileType == 'unknown') {
        return SaveResult(success: false, error: 'Unsupported file type');
      }

      final Directory appDir = await getApplicationDocumentsDirectory();
      final String basePath = path.join(appDir.path, 'secure_documents');
      final String subFolder = fileType == 'pdf' ? 'pdfs' : 'images';
      final String folderPath = path.join(basePath, subFolder);
      final Directory targetDir = Directory(folderPath);

      if (!await targetDir.exists()) {
        await targetDir.create(recursive: true);
      }

      final String timestamp = DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch.toString();
      final String fileName = '${categoryId}_$timestamp$fileExtension';
      final String filePath = path.join(folderPath, fileName);

      final fileBytes = await imageFile.readAsBytes();

      File savedFile;
      bool isEncrypted = false;

      if (isEncryptionReady) {
        final encryptedBytes = await _encryptFileContent(fileBytes);
        savedFile = await File(filePath).writeAsBytes(encryptedBytes);
        isEncrypted = true;
        debugPrint('âœ… File encrypted');
      } else {
        savedFile = await imageFile.copy(filePath);
        debugPrint('âš ï¸ Saved without encryption');
      }

      if (!await savedFile.exists()) {
        return SaveResult(success: false, error: 'Failed to save');
      }

      final int fileSize = await savedFile.length();

      final DocumentItem document = DocumentItem(
        id: timestamp,
        name: documentName,
        categoryId: categoryId,
        addedAt: DateTime.now(),
        thumbnailPath: filePath,
        fileSize: fileSize,
        fileType: fileType,
        isEncrypted: isEncrypted,
      );

      final bool metadataSaved = await _saveMetadata(document);
      if (!metadataSaved) {
        await savedFile.delete();
        return SaveResult(success: false, error: 'Failed to save metadata');
      }

      return SaveResult(
        success: true,
        document: document,
        savedPath: filePath,
        fileType: fileType,
      );
    } catch (e) {
      return SaveResult(success: false, error: 'Error: ${e.toString()}');
    }
  }

  Future<File?> getDecryptedDocumentFile(DocumentItem document) async {
    try {
      if (document.thumbnailPath == null) return null;

      final originalFile = File(document.thumbnailPath!);
      if (!await originalFile.exists()) return null;

      if (!document.isEncrypted) return originalFile;

      if (!isEncryptionReady) {
        debugPrint('âŒ Encryption not initialized');
        return null;
      }

      final encryptedBytes = await originalFile.readAsBytes();
      final decryptedBytes = await _decryptFileContent(encryptedBytes);

      final tempDir = await getTemporaryDirectory();
      final ext = path.extension(document.thumbnailPath!);
      final tempPath = path.join(tempDir.path, 'decrypted_${document.id}$ext');
      final tempFile = File(tempPath);
      await tempFile.writeAsBytes(decryptedBytes);

      debugPrint('âœ… Decrypted');
      return tempFile;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Error: $e');
      return null;
    }
  }

  String _detectFileType(String extension) {
    switch (extension) {
      case '.jpg':
      case '.jpeg':
      case '.png':
      case '.gif':
      case '.bmp':
      case '.webp':
        return 'image';
      case '.pdf':
        return 'pdf';
      default:
        return 'unknown';
    }
  }

  Future<bool> _saveMetadata(DocumentItem document) async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final List<DocumentItem> documents = await getAllDocuments();
      documents.add(document);
      final List<String> jsonList = documents
          .map((doc) => jsonEncode(doc.toJson()))
          .toList();
      return await prefs.setStringList(_documentsKey, jsonList);
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<List<DocumentItem>> getAllDocuments() async {
    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final List<String>? jsonList = prefs.getStringList(_documentsKey);
      if (jsonList == null || jsonList.isEmpty) return [];
      return jsonList
          .map((jsonStr) => DocumentItem.fromJson(jsonDecode(jsonStr)))
          .toList();
    } catch (e) {
      return [];
    }
  }

  Future<List<DocumentItem>> getRecentDocuments({int limit = 5}) async {
    final documents = await getAllDocuments();
    documents.sort((a, b) => b.addedAt.compareTo(a.addedAt));
    return documents.take(limit).toList();
  }

  Future<int> getDocumentCount() async {
    final documents = await getAllDocuments();
    return documents.length;
  }

  Future<int> getTotalStorageUsed() async {
    final documents = await getAllDocuments();
    return documents.fold<int>(0, (sum, doc) => sum + doc.fileSize);
  }

  Future<List<DocumentItem>> getDocumentsByCategory(String categoryId) async {
    final documents = await getAllDocuments();
    return documents.where((doc) => doc.categoryId == categoryId).toList();
  }

  Future<int> getCategoryDocumentCount(String categoryId) async {
    final documents = await getDocumentsByCategory(categoryId);
    return documents.length;
  }

  Future<bool> renameDocument(String documentId, String newName) async {
    try {
      if (newName.trim().isEmpty) return false;
      final documents = await getAllDocuments();
      final index = documents.indexWhere((doc) => doc.id == documentId);
      if (index == -1) return false;

      final oldDoc = documents[index];
      final updatedDoc = DocumentItem(
        id: oldDoc.id,
        name: newName.trim(),
        categoryId: oldDoc.categoryId,
        addedAt: oldDoc.addedAt,
        thumbnailPath: oldDoc.thumbnailPath,
        fileSize: oldDoc.fileSize,
        fileType: oldDoc.fileType,
        isEncrypted: oldDoc.isEncrypted,
      );

      documents[index] = updatedDoc;
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final List<String> jsonList = documents
          .map((doc) => jsonEncode(doc.toJson()))
          .toList();
      return await prefs.setStringList(_documentsKey, jsonList);
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<bool> deleteDocument(String documentId) async {
    try {
      final documents = await getAllDocuments();
      final docIndex = documents.indexWhere((doc) => doc.id == documentId);
      if (docIndex == -1) return false;

      final document = documents[docIndex];
      if (document.thumbnailPath != null && document.thumbnailPath!.isNotEmpty) {
        try {
          final File file = File(document.thumbnailPath!);
          if (await file.exists()) await file.delete();
        } catch (e) {
          debugPrint('Warning: ${e.toString()}');
        }
      }

      documents.removeAt(docIndex);
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final List<String> jsonList = documents
          .map((doc) => jsonEncode(doc.toJson()))
          .toList();
      return await prefs.setStringList(_documentsKey, jsonList);
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<bool> moveDocumentToCategory(String documentId, String newCategoryId) async {
    try {
      final documents = await getAllDocuments();
      final index = documents.indexWhere((doc) => doc.id == documentId);
      if (index == -1) return false;

      final oldDoc = documents[index];
      final updatedDoc = DocumentItem(
        id: oldDoc.id,
        name: oldDoc.name,
        categoryId: newCategoryId,
        addedAt: oldDoc.addedAt,
        thumbnailPath: oldDoc.thumbnailPath,
        fileSize: oldDoc.fileSize,
        fileType: oldDoc.fileType,
        isEncrypted: oldDoc.isEncrypted,
      );

      documents[index] = updatedDoc;
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      final List<String> jsonList = documents
          .map((doc) => jsonEncode(doc.toJson()))
          .toList();
      return await prefs.setStringList(_documentsKey, jsonList);
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  Future<List<DocumentItem>> searchDocuments(String query, [String? categoryId]) async {
    try {
      if (query.trim().isEmpty) return [];
      final documents = await getAllDocuments();
      final searchQuery = query.toLowerCase().trim();

      var results = documents.where((doc) {
        final docName = doc.name.toLowerCase();
        return docName.contains(searchQuery);
      }).toList();

      if (categoryId != null && categoryId.isNotEmpty) {
        results = results.where((doc) => doc.categoryId == categoryId).toList();
      }

      results.sort((a, b) {
        final aName = a.name.toLowerCase();
        final bName = b.name.toLowerCase();
        if (aName == searchQuery && bName != searchQuery) return -1;
        if (aName != searchQuery && bName == searchQuery) return 1;
        return b.addedAt.compareTo(a.addedAt);
      });

      return results;
    } catch (e) {
      return [];
    }
  }

  void debugPrint(String message) {
    print('ğŸ“¦ DocumentStorage: $message');
  }
}

class SaveResult {
  final bool success;
  final DocumentItem? document;
  final String? savedPath;
  final String? fileType;
  final String? error;

  SaveResult({
    required this.success,
    this.document,
    this.savedPath,
    this.fileType,
    this.error,
  });
}
```

### File 48: gallery_service.dart

```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:image_picker/image_picker.dart';
import 'package:permission_handler/permission_handler.dart';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart' show kIsWeb;

class GalleryService {
  static final GalleryService _instance = GalleryService._internal();
  factory GalleryService() => _instance;
  GalleryService._internal();

  final ImagePicker _picker = ImagePicker();

  /// 1. Gallery permission check & request (Android 13+ compatible)
  Future<bool> requestGalleryPermission() async {
    // Windows aur Web pe gallery permission ki zarurat nahi
    if (Platform.isWindows || kIsWeb) {
      return true;
    }

    try {
      // Android 13+ (API 33+) ke liye READ_MEDIA_IMAGES
      if (Platform.isAndroid) {
        final androidInfo = await _getAndroidVersion();

        if (androidInfo >= 33) {
          // Android 13+ - Use READ_MEDIA_IMAGES
          final status = await Permission.photos.status;

          if (status.isGranted) {
            return true;
          }

          if (status.isDenied) {
            final result = await Permission.photos.request();
            return result.isGranted;
          }

          // Permanently denied - settings me bhejo
          if (status.isPermanentlyDenied) {
            await openAppSettings();
            return false;
          }
        } else {
          // Android 12 aur niche - Use READ_EXTERNAL_STORAGE
          final status = await Permission.storage.status;

          if (status.isGranted) {
            return true;
          }

          if (status.isDenied) {
            final result = await Permission.storage.request();
            return result.isGranted;
          }

          if (status.isPermanentlyDenied) {
            await openAppSettings();
            return false;
          }
        }
      }

      // iOS ke liye photos permission
      if (Platform.isIOS) {
        final status = await Permission.photos.status;

        if (status.isGranted || status.isLimited) {
          return true;
        }

        if (status.isDenied) {
          final result = await Permission.photos.request();
          return result.isGranted || result.isLimited;
        }

        if (status.isPermanentlyDenied) {
          await openAppSettings();
          return false;
        }
      }

      return false;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// Android version check helper
  Future<int> _getAndroidVersion() async {
    if (!Platform.isAndroid) return 0;

    try {
      // Android SDK version nikalne ke liye
      // Yeh simple approach hai - production me device_info_plus use karo
      return 33; // Default assume Android 13+
    } catch (e) {
      return 30; // Fallback
    }
  }

  /// 2. Check if gallery is available
  Future<bool> isGalleryAvailable() async {
    // Windows pe gallery picker available nahi hai by default
    if (Platform.isWindows) {
      return false;
    }

    try {
      final status = await Permission.photos.status;
      return status.isGranted || status.isDenied;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// 3. Main method: Pick image from gallery
  Future<GalleryResult> pickFromGallery() async {
    try {
      // Windows platform check - crash prevent karne ke liye
      if (Platform.isWindows) {
        return GalleryResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Gallery picker is not available on Windows platform.',
        );
      }

      // Step 1: Permission check
      final permissionGranted = await requestGalleryPermission();

      if (!permissionGranted) {
        return GalleryResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Gallery permission denied. Please enable it in settings.',
        );
      }

      // Step 2: Open gallery and pick image
      final XFile? image = await _picker.pickImage(
        source: ImageSource.gallery,
        imageQuality: 85, // Compress to reduce file size
        maxWidth: 1920,
        maxHeight: 1920,
      );

      // Step 3: Handle cancellation
      if (image == null) {
        return GalleryResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Image selection cancelled',
        );
      }

      // Step 4: Validate file
      final File imageFile = File(image.path);

      if (!await imageFile.exists()) {
        return GalleryResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Selected file not found',
        );
      }

      final fileSize = await imageFile.length();

      if (fileSize == 0) {
        return GalleryResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Selected file is empty',
        );
      }

      // Step 5: Return success with file
      return GalleryResult(
        success: true,
        imageFile: imageFile,
        xFile: image,
      );

    } catch (e) {
      return GalleryResult(
        success: false,
        error: 'Failed to pick image: ${e.toString()}',
      );
    }
  }

  /// Pick multiple images (future enhancement)
  Future<List<GalleryResult>> pickMultipleImages() async {
    try {
      if (Platform.isWindows) {
        return [
          GalleryResult(
            success: false,
            error: 'Gallery picker is not available on Windows platform.',
          )
        ];
      }

      final permissionGranted = await requestGalleryPermission();

      if (!permissionGranted) {
        return [
          GalleryResult(
            success: false,
            error: 'Gallery permission denied.',
          )
        ];
      }

      final List<XFile> images = await _picker.pickMultiImage(
        imageQuality: 85,
        maxWidth: 1920,
        maxHeight: 1920,
      );

      if (images.isEmpty) {
        return [
          GalleryResult(
            success: false,
            error: 'No images selected',
          )
        ];
      }

      return images.map((xFile) {
        return GalleryResult(
          success: true,
          imageFile: File(xFile.path),
          xFile: xFile,
        );
      }).toList();

    } catch (e) {
      return [
        GalleryResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Failed to pick images: ${e.toString()}',
        )
      ];
    }
  }
}

/// Result model for gallery operations
class GalleryResult {
  final bool success;
  final File? imageFile;
  final XFile? xFile;
  final String? error;

  GalleryResult({
    required this.success,
    this.imageFile,
    this.xFile,
    this.error,
  });
}
```

```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:file_picker/file_picker.dart';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart' show kIsWeb;

class PdfPickerService {
  static final PdfPickerService _instance = PdfPickerService._internal();
  factory PdfPickerService() => _instance;
  PdfPickerService._internal();

  /// Main method: Pick PDF from file system
  Future<PdfPickResult> pickPdf() async {
    try {
      // Step 1: Platform check - Web pe alag handling ho sakti hai
      if (kIsWeb) {
        return PdfPickResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'PDF picker is not fully supported on web platform.',
        );
      }

      // Step 2: Open file picker with PDF filter
      FilePickerResult? result = await FilePicker.platform.pickFiles(
        type: FileType.custom,
        allowedExtensions: ['pdf'],
        allowMultiple: false,
      );

      // Step 3: Handle cancellation
      if (result == null) {
        return PdfPickResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'PDF selection cancelled',
        );
      }

      // Step 4: Get the picked file
      if (result.files.isEmpty) {
        return PdfPickResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'No file selected',
        );
      }

      final PlatformFile platformFile = result.files.first;

      // Step 5: Validate file extension
      if (platformFile.extension?.toLowerCase() != 'pdf') {
        return PdfPickResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Selected file is not a PDF. Please select a .pdf file.',
        );
      }

      // Step 6: Get file path
      final String? filePath = platformFile.path;

      if (filePath == null) {
        return PdfPickResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Could not access file path',
        );
      }

      // Step 7: Create File object
      final File pdfFile = File(filePath);

      // Step 8: Validate file exists
      if (!await pdfFile.exists()) {
        return PdfPickResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Selected PDF file not found',
        );
      }

      // Step 9: Validate file size (0 bytes check)
      final fileSize = await pdfFile.length();

      if (fileSize == 0) {
        return PdfPickResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'Selected PDF file is empty (0 bytes)',
        );
      }

      // Optional: Max file size check (50 MB)
      const int maxFileSizeBytes = 50 * 1024 * 1024; // 50 MB
      if (fileSize > maxFileSizeBytes) {
        return PdfPickResult(
          success: false,
          error: 'PDF file is too large. Maximum size is 50 MB.',
        );
      }

      // Step 10: Return success with file
      return PdfPickResult(
        success: true,
        pdfFile: pdfFile,
        fileName: platformFile.name,
        fileSize: fileSize,
      );

    } catch (e) {
      return PdfPickResult(
        success: false,
        error: 'Failed to pick PDF: ${e.toString()}',
      );
    }
  }

  /// Check if file picker is available on platform
  Future<bool> isPickerAvailable() async {
    try {
      // Web pe limited support hai
      if (kIsWeb) {
        return false;
      }

      // Mobile aur desktop platforms pe available hai
      if (Platform.isAndroid || Platform.isIOS || Platform.isWindows || Platform.isMacOS || Platform.isLinux) {
        return true;
      }

      return false;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// Helper: Get formatted file size
  String getFormattedFileSize(int bytes) {
    if (bytes < 1024) {
      return '$bytes B';
    } else if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) {
      return '${(bytes / 1024).toStringAsFixed(1)} KB';
    } else {
      return '${(bytes / (1024 * 1024)).toStringAsFixed(1)} MB';
    }
  }
}

/// Result model for PDF picker operations
class PdfPickResult {
  final bool success;
  final File? pdfFile;
  final String? fileName;
  final int? fileSize;
  final String? error;

  PdfPickResult({
    required this.success,
    this.pdfFile,
    this.fileName,
    this.fileSize,
    this.error,
  });

  /// Helper method to get formatted file size
  String get formattedFileSize {
    if (fileSize == null) return '0 B';

    if (fileSize! < 1024) {
      return '$fileSize B';
    } else if (fileSize! < 1024 * 1024) {
      return '${(fileSize! / 1024).toStringAsFixed(1)} KB';
    } else {
      return '${(fileSize! / (1024 * 1024)).toStringAsFixed(1)} MB';
    }
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'dart:io' show Platform;
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart' show kIsWeb;

// âœ… FIX: Import the implementations
import 'secure_storage_service_stub.dart';
import 'secure_storage_service_real.dart';

// This file acts as a facade to choose the right implementation
class SecureStorageServiceFactory {
  static SecureStorageService create() {
    // Check if running on Windows
    if (!kIsWeb && Platform.isWindows) {
      // Return stub implementation for Windows
      return SecureStorageServiceStub();
    } else {
      // Return real implementation for other platforms
      return SecureStorageServiceReal();
    }
  }
}

// Abstract interface
abstract class SecureStorageService {
  Future<bool> savePin(String pin);
  Future<PinVerificationResult> verifyPin(String pin);
  Future<bool> get isPinSet;
  Future<void> setBiometricEnabled(bool enabled);
  Future<bool> get isBiometricEnabled;

}

class PinVerificationResult {
  final bool success;
  final bool isLocked;
  final int? remainingSeconds;
  final int? attemptsLeft;
  final int? currentAttempts;
  final String? errorMessage;

  PinVerificationResult({
    required this.success,
    required this.isLocked,
    this.remainingSeconds,
    this.attemptsLeft,
    this.currentAttempts,
    this.errorMessage,
  });
}

class PinLockStatus {

  final int? remainingSeconds;
  final DateTime? lockUntil;

    required this.isLocked,
    this.remainingSeconds,
    this.lockUntil,
```

### File 51: secure_storage_service_real.dart
**Path:** `lib\core\services\secure_storage_service_real.dart`
**Size:** 6.47 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter_secure_storage/flutter_secure_storage.dart';
import 'dart:convert';
import 'dart:math';
import 'dart:typed_data';
import 'package:crypto/crypto.dart';
import 'secure_storage_service.dart';

class SecureStorageServiceReal implements SecureStorageService {
  static final SecureStorageServiceReal _instance = SecureStorageServiceReal._internal();

  factory SecureStorageServiceReal() => _instance;
  SecureStorageServiceReal._internal();

  final FlutterSecureStorage _storage = const FlutterSecureStorage(
    aOptions: AndroidOptions(
      encryptedSharedPreferences: true,
    ),
  );

  // Storage keys
  static const String _pinKey = 'user_pin';
  static const String _saltKey = 'pin_salt';
  static const String _biometricEnabledKey = 'biometric_enabled';
  static const String _wrongAttemptsKey = 'wrong_attempts';
  static const String _lockTimeKey = 'lock_time';

  // PBKDF2 configuration
  static const int iterations = 100000;
  static const int keyLength = 32;
  static const int saltLength = 16;
  static const int maxAttempts = 5;
  static const int lockDurationSeconds = 30;

  /// Generate cryptographically secure random salt
  String _generateSalt() {
    final random = Random.secure();
    final saltBytes = Uint8List(saltLength);
    for (int i = 0; i < saltLength; i++) {
      saltBytes[i] = random.nextInt(256);
    }
    return base64Encode(saltBytes);
  }

  /// Derive key using PBKDF2
  String _deriveKey(String pin, String salt) {
    final saltBytes = base64Decode(salt);
    final pinBytes = utf8.encode(pin);

    var hash = Hmac(sha256, saltBytes).convert(pinBytes).bytes;
    for (int i = 1; i < iterations; i++) {
      hash = Hmac(sha256, saltBytes).convert(hash).bytes;
    }

    return base64Encode(Uint8List.fromList(hash.take(keyLength).toList()));
  }

  @override
  Future<bool> savePin(String pin) async {
    try {
      final salt = _generateSalt();
      final derivedKey = _deriveKey(pin, salt);

      await _storage.write(key: _saltKey, value: salt);
      await _storage.write(key: _pinKey, value: derivedKey);

      return true;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  @override
  Future<PinVerificationResult> verifyPin(String pin) async {
    try {
      final lockStatus = await _checkLockStatus();
      if (lockStatus.isLocked) {
        return PinVerificationResult(
          success: false,
          isLocked: true,
          remainingSeconds: lockStatus.remainingSeconds,
          attemptsLeft: 0,
          errorMessage: 'App locked for ${lockStatus.remainingSeconds}s',
        );
      }

      final storedKey = await _storage.read(key: _pinKey);
      final salt = await _storage.read(key: _saltKey);

      if (storedKey == null || salt == null) {
        return PinVerificationResult(
          success: false,
          isLocked: false,
          errorMessage: 'PIN not set',
        );
      }

      final derivedKey = _deriveKey(pin, salt);
      final isValid = storedKey == derivedKey;

      if (isValid) {
        await _resetWrongAttempts();
        await _clearLockTime();
        return PinVerificationResult(success: true, isLocked: false);
      } else {
        await _incrementWrongAttempts();
        final attempts = await _getWrongAttempts();
        final attemptsLeft = maxAttempts - attempts;

        if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
          final lockTime = DateTime.now().add(Duration(seconds: lockDurationSeconds));
          await _setLockTime(lockTime);
          return PinVerificationResult(
            success: false,
            isLocked: true,
            remainingSeconds: lockDurationSeconds,
            attemptsLeft: 0,
            errorMessage: 'Too many attempts. Locked for $lockDurationSeconds seconds.',
          );
        }

        return PinVerificationResult(
          success: false,
          isLocked: false,
          attemptsLeft: attemptsLeft,
          currentAttempts: attempts,
          errorMessage: 'Wrong PIN! $attemptsLeft attempts left.',
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      return PinVerificationResult(
        success: false,
        isLocked: false,
        errorMessage: 'Verification error: ${e.toString()}',
      );
    }
  }

  Future<PinLockStatus> _checkLockStatus() async {
    final lockTimeStr = await _storage.read(key: _lockTimeKey);
    if (lockTimeStr == null) {
      return PinLockStatus(isLocked: false);
    }

    final lockTime = DateTime.tryParse(lockTimeStr);
    if (lockTime == null) {
      return PinLockStatus(isLocked: false);
    }

    final now = DateTime.now();
    if (now.isBefore(lockTime)) {
      final remainingSeconds = lockTime.difference(now).inSeconds;
      return PinLockStatus(
        isLocked: true,
        remainingSeconds: remainingSeconds,
        lockUntil: lockTime,
      );
    } else {
      await _clearLockTime();
      await _resetWrongAttempts();
      return PinLockStatus(isLocked: false);
    }
  }

  @override
  Future<bool> get isPinSet async {
    final pin = await _storage.read(key: _pinKey);
    final salt = await _storage.read(key: _saltKey);
    return pin != null && salt != null;
  }

  Future<void> _incrementWrongAttempts() async {
    final attempts = await _getWrongAttempts();
    await _storage.write(key: _wrongAttemptsKey, value: (attempts + 1).toString());
  }

  Future<int> _getWrongAttempts() async {
    final attemptsStr = await _storage.read(key: _wrongAttemptsKey);
    return int.tryParse(attemptsStr ?? '0') ?? 0;
  }

  Future<void> _resetWrongAttempts() async {
    await _storage.delete(key: _wrongAttemptsKey);
  }

  Future<void> _setLockTime(DateTime time) async {
    await _storage.write(key: _lockTimeKey, value: time.toIso8601String());
  }

  Future<void> _clearLockTime() async {
    await _storage.delete(key: _lockTimeKey);
  }

  @override
  Future<void> setBiometricEnabled(bool enabled) async {
    await _storage.write(key: _biometricEnabledKey, value: enabled.toString());
  }

  @override
  Future<bool> get isBiometricEnabled async {
    final value = await _storage.read(key: _biometricEnabledKey);
    return value == 'true';
  }

  @override
  Future<void> clearPin() async {
    await _storage.delete(key: _pinKey);
    await _storage.delete(key: _saltKey);
    await _resetWrongAttempts();
    await _clearLockTime();
  }

  @override
  Future<void> resetAll() async {
    await _storage.deleteAll();
  }
}

```

### File 52: secure_storage_service_stub.dart

```dart
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart' show kIsWeb;
import 'dart:io' show Platform;
import 'secure_storage_service.dart';

class SecureStorageServiceStub implements SecureStorageService {
  static final SecureStorageServiceStub _instance = SecureStorageServiceStub._internal();

  factory SecureStorageServiceStub() => _instance;
  SecureStorageServiceStub._internal() {
    if (_isWindows) {
      print('âš ï¸ â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•');
      print('âš ï¸  WARNING: Windows Stub Mode Active!');
      print('âš ï¸  Data stored in MEMORY ONLY - NOT SECURE');
      print('âš ï¸  For production: Install ATL in Visual Studio');
      print('âš ï¸ â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•');
    }
  }

  // In-memory storage (NOT SECURE)
  final Map<String, String> _memoryStorage = {};

  // Storage keys
  static const String _pinKey = 'user_pin';
  static const String _saltKey = 'pin_salt';
  static const String _biometricEnabledKey = 'biometric_enabled';
  static const String _wrongAttemptsKey = 'wrong_attempts';
  static const String _lockTimeKey = 'lock_time';

  // Configuration
  static const int maxAttempts = 5;
  static const int lockDurationSeconds = 30;

  bool get _isWindows => !kIsWeb && Platform.isWindows;

  String _generateSalt() {
    return DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch.toString();
  }

  String _deriveKey(String pin, String salt) {
    return '$pin:$salt'.hashCode.toString();
  }

  @override
  Future<bool> savePin(String pin) async {
    try {
      final salt = _generateSalt();
      final derivedKey = _deriveKey(pin, salt);

      _memoryStorage[_saltKey] = salt;
      _memoryStorage[_pinKey] = derivedKey;

      print('âœ… PIN saved (Windows stub mode)');
      return true;
    } catch (e) {
      print('âŒ Error saving PIN: $e');
      return false;
    }
  }

  @override
  Future<PinVerificationResult> verifyPin(String pin) async {
    try {
      final lockStatus = await _checkLockStatus();
      if (lockStatus.isLocked) {
        return PinVerificationResult(
          success: false,
          isLocked: true,
          remainingSeconds: lockStatus.remainingSeconds,
          attemptsLeft: 0,
          errorMessage: 'App locked for ${lockStatus.remainingSeconds}s',
        );
      }

      final storedKey = _memoryStorage[_pinKey];
      final salt = _memoryStorage[_saltKey];

      if (storedKey == null || salt == null) {
        return PinVerificationResult(
          success: false,
          isLocked: false,
          errorMessage: 'PIN not set',
        );
      }

      final derivedKey = _deriveKey(pin, salt);
      final isValid = storedKey == derivedKey;

      if (isValid) {
        await _resetWrongAttempts();
        await _clearLockTime();
        return PinVerificationResult(success: true, isLocked: false);
      } else {
        await _incrementWrongAttempts();
        final attempts = await _getWrongAttempts();
        final attemptsLeft = maxAttempts - attempts;

        if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
          final lockTime = DateTime.now().add(Duration(seconds: lockDurationSeconds));
          await _setLockTime(lockTime);
          return PinVerificationResult(
            success: false,
            isLocked: true,
            remainingSeconds: lockDurationSeconds,
            attemptsLeft: 0,
            errorMessage: 'Too many attempts. Locked for $lockDurationSeconds seconds.',
          );
        }

        return PinVerificationResult(
          success: false,
          isLocked: false,
          attemptsLeft: attemptsLeft,
          currentAttempts: attempts,
          errorMessage: 'Wrong PIN! $attemptsLeft attempts left.',
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      return PinVerificationResult(
        success: false,
        isLocked: false,
        errorMessage: 'Verification error: ${e.toString()}',
      );
    }
  }

  Future<PinLockStatus> _checkLockStatus() async {
    final lockTimeStr = _memoryStorage[_lockTimeKey];
    if (lockTimeStr == null) {
      return PinLockStatus(isLocked: false);
    }

    final lockTime = DateTime.tryParse(lockTimeStr);
    if (lockTime == null) {
      return PinLockStatus(isLocked: false);
    }

    final now = DateTime.now();
    if (now.isBefore(lockTime)) {
      final remainingSeconds = lockTime.difference(now).inSeconds;
      return PinLockStatus(
        isLocked: true,
        remainingSeconds: remainingSeconds,
        lockUntil: lockTime,
      );
    } else {
      await _clearLockTime();
      await _resetWrongAttempts();
      return PinLockStatus(isLocked: false);
    }
  }

  @override
  Future<bool> get isPinSet async {
    return _memoryStorage[_pinKey] != null && _memoryStorage[_saltKey] != null;
  }

  Future<void> _incrementWrongAttempts() async {
    final attempts = await _getWrongAttempts();
    _memoryStorage[_wrongAttemptsKey] = (attempts + 1).toString();
  }

  Future<int> _getWrongAttempts() async {
    return int.tryParse(_memoryStorage[_wrongAttemptsKey] ?? '0') ?? 0;
  }

  Future<void> _resetWrongAttempts() async {
    _memoryStorage.remove(_wrongAttemptsKey);
  }

  Future<void> _setLockTime(DateTime time) async {
    _memoryStorage[_lockTimeKey] = time.toIso8601String();
  }

  Future<void> _clearLockTime() async {
    _memoryStorage.remove(_lockTimeKey);
  }

  @override
  Future<void> setBiometricEnabled(bool enabled) async {
    _memoryStorage[_biometricEnabledKey] = enabled.toString();
  }

  @override
  Future<bool> get isBiometricEnabled async {
    return _memoryStorage[_biometricEnabledKey] == 'true';
  }

  @override
  Future<void> clearPin() async {
    _memoryStorage.remove(_pinKey);
    _memoryStorage.remove(_saltKey);
    await _resetWrongAttempts();
    await _clearLockTime();
  }

  @override
  Future<void> resetAll() async {
    _memoryStorage.clear();
    print('âœ… All data cleared (Windows stub mode)');
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../core/services/secure_storage_service.dart';
import '../../core/services/biometric_service.dart';
import '../../core/services/app_lifecycle_service.dart';
import 'widgets/pin_input_row.dart';
import '../documents/documents_screen.dart';

class PinSetupScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final bool isSetupMode;

  const PinSetupScreen({
    super.key,
    this.isSetupMode = true,
  });

  @override
  State<PinSetupScreen> createState() => _PinSetupScreenState();
}

class _PinSetupScreenState extends State<PinSetupScreen> {
  final _secureStorage = SecureStorageServiceFactory.create();
  final _biometric = BiometricService();
  final _lifecycleService = AppLifecycleService();

  String _enteredPin = '';
  bool _isPinComplete = false;
  bool _isLoading = false;
  String _errorMessage = '';
  bool _biometricAvailable = false;
  DateTime? _lockUntil;
  int _pinResetCounter = 0;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _checkBiometricAvailability();
  }

  /// âœ… UPDATED: Check biometric availability for BOTH modes
  Future<void> _checkBiometricAvailability() async {
    final available = await _biometric.isBiometricAvailable();

    if (widget.isSetupMode) {
      // âœ… SETUP MODE: Show button if hardware available (even if not enabled yet)
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _biometricAvailable = available;
        });
      }
    } else {
      // âœ… VERIFY MODE: Show button only if enabled AND available
      final enabled = await _secureStorage.isBiometricEnabled;
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _biometricAvailable = available && enabled;
        });
      }
    }
  }

  void _onPinChanged(String pin) {
    setState(() {
      _enteredPin = pin;
      _isPinComplete = pin.length == 6;
      _errorMessage = '';
    });

    if (_isPinComplete) {
      Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 300), () {
        if (mounted) _handlePinComplete();
      });
    }
  }

  Future<void> _handlePinComplete() async {
    if (widget.isSetupMode) {
      await _handleSetupMode();
    } else {
      await _handleVerifyMode();
    }
  }

  /// âœ… Direct save without confirm
  Future<void> _handleSetupMode() async {
    setState(() => _isLoading = true);

    final saved = await _secureStorage.savePin(_enteredPin);

    if (saved) {
      await _lifecycleService.authenticateUser();

      if (await _biometric.isBiometricAvailable()) {
        if (mounted) _showBiometricSetupDialog();
      } else {
        if (mounted) _navigateToHome();
      }
    } else {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _errorMessage = 'Failed to save PIN. Try again.';
          _isLoading = false;
          _isPinComplete = false;
          _enteredPin = '';
          _pinResetCounter++;
        });
      }
    }
  }

  Future<void> _handleVerifyMode() async {
    if (_lockUntil != null) return;

    setState(() => _isLoading = true);

    final result = await _secureStorage.verifyPin(_enteredPin);

    if (result.success) {
      await _lifecycleService.authenticateUser();
      if (mounted) _navigateToHome();
    } else if (result.isLocked) {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _isLoading = false;
          _lockUntil = DateTime.now().add(Duration(seconds: result.remainingSeconds ?? 30));
          _errorMessage = result.errorMessage ?? 'App is locked';
        });
        _showLockDialog();
      }
    } else {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _isLoading = false;
          _isPinComplete = false;
          _enteredPin = '';
          _pinResetCounter++;
          _errorMessage = result.errorMessage ?? 'Wrong PIN';
        });
      }
    }
  }

  /// âœ… UPDATED: Handle biometric in BOTH modes
  Future<void> _onBiometricLogin() async {
    if (!_biometricAvailable || _lockUntil != null) return;

    if (widget.isSetupMode) {
      // âœ… SETUP MODE: Direct enable + save + navigate
      setState(() => _isLoading = true);

      final result = await _biometric.authenticate();

      if (mounted) {
        setState(() => _isLoading = false);

        if (result.success) {
          // Enable biometric immediately
          await _secureStorage.setBiometricEnabled(true);

          setState(() {
            _errorMessage = 'âœ… Biometric enabled! Now create your PIN.';
          });

          // Show success message for 2 seconds
          await Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 2));

          if (mounted) {
            setState(() {
              _errorMessage = '';
            });
          }
        } else {
          setState(() {
            _errorMessage = result.error ?? 'Biometric setup failed';
          });
        }
      }
    } else {
      // âœ… VERIFY MODE: Authenticate and navigate
      setState(() => _isLoading = true);

      final result = await _biometric.authenticate();

      if (mounted) {
        setState(() => _isLoading = false);

        if (result.success) {
          await _lifecycleService.authenticateUser();
          if (mounted) _navigateToHome();
        } else {
          setState(() {
            _errorMessage = result.error ?? 'Biometric authentication failed';
          });
        }
      }
    }
  }

  void _navigateToHome() {
    Navigator.pushReplacement(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const DocumentsScreen()),
    );
  }

  void _showBiometricSetupDialog() {
    showDialog(
      context: context,
      barrierDismissible: false,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        backgroundColor: AppColors.white,
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16)),
        title: const Text(
          'Enable Biometric Login?',
          style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.primary, fontWeight: FontWeight.w700),
        ),
        content: const Text(
          'Use fingerprint or face recognition for faster secure access?',
          style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.textSecondary),
        ),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () {
              Navigator.pop(context);
              _navigateToHome();
            },
            child: const Text('Skip', style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.textSecondary)),
          ),
          ElevatedButton(
            style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
              backgroundColor: AppColors.accentCyan,
              foregroundColor: AppColors.white,
              shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8)),
            ),
            onPressed: () async {
              await _secureStorage.setBiometricEnabled(true);
              if (mounted) {
                Navigator.pop(context);
                _navigateToHome();
              }
            },
            child: const Text('Enable'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showLockDialog() {
    showDialog(
      context: context,
      barrierDismissible: false,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        backgroundColor: AppColors.white,
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16)),
        icon: const Icon(Icons.lock_clock, size: 48, color: AppColors.error),
        title: const Text(
          'App Locked',
          style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.error, fontWeight: FontWeight.w700),
        ),
        content: Text(
          _errorMessage.isNotEmpty
              ? _errorMessage
              : 'Too many wrong attempts. Please try again later.',
          textAlign: TextAlign.center,
          style: const TextStyle(color: AppColors.textSecondary),
        ),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
            child: const Text('OK'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  void _onForgotPin() {
    showDialog(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        backgroundColor: AppColors.white,
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16)),
        title: const Text(
          'Forgot PIN?',
          style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.primary, fontWeight: FontWeight.w700),
        ),
        content: const Text(
          'You will need to reinstall the app to reset your PIN. All data will be lost.',
          style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.textSecondary),
        ),
```
