```dart
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
            child: const Text('Cancel'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

        ? 'Create PIN'
        : 'Secure Your Vault';

    String subtitle = widget.isSetupMode
        ? 'Create a 6-digit PIN for security'
        : 'Enter your 6-digit PIN to access protected documents.';

    return Column(
      children: [
        Container(
          width: 80,
          height: 80,

            shape: BoxShape.circle,
            color: AppColors.transparentCyan10,

        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 24),
        Text(
          title,
          style: const TextStyle(

          ),

              fontWeight: FontWeight.w400,
              height: 1.4,

  }

  Widget _buildError() {
    // âœ… Different styling for success vs error messages
    final isSuccess = _errorMessage.startsWith('âœ…');

    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 32, vertical: 16),

        decoration: BoxDecoration(

              : AppColors.error.withValues(alpha: 0.15),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
          border: Border.all(
            color: isSuccess
                ? AppColors.success.withValues(alpha: 0.3)
                : AppColors.error.withValues(alpha: 0.3),
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';

class PinInputRow extends StatefulWidget {
  final ValueChanged<String> onPinChanged;

  const PinInputRow({
    super.key,
    required this.onPinChanged,
  });

  @override
  State<PinInputRow> createState() => PinInputRowState();
}

class PinInputRowState extends State<PinInputRow> {
  late List<TextEditingController> controllers;
  late List<FocusNode> focusNodes;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    controllers = List.generate(6, (_) => TextEditingController());
    focusNodes = List.generate(6, (_) => FocusNode());
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    for (var controller in controllers) {
      controller.dispose();
    }
    for (var node in focusNodes) {
      node.dispose();
    }
    super.dispose();
  }

  void onChanged(int index, String value) {
    if (value.isNotEmpty) {
      if (index < 5) {
        focusNodes[index + 1].requestFocus();
      }
    } else if (value.isEmpty) {
      if (index > 0) {
        focusNodes[index - 1].requestFocus();
      }
    }
    notifyPinChange();
  }

  void notifyPinChange() {
    final pin = controllers.map((c) => c.text).join();
    widget.onPinChanged(pin);
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return SingleChildScrollView(  // âœ… FIX: Added scrolling
      scrollDirection: Axis.horizontal,
      child: Padding(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12),  // âœ… Reduced from 20
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: List.generate(
            6,
                (index) => Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 4),  // âœ… Reduced
              child: buildPinBox(index),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget buildPinBox(int index) {
    return SizedBox(
      width: 44,  // âœ… Reduced from 48
      height: 56,
      child: TextField(
        controller: controllers[index],
        focusNode: focusNodes[index],
        textAlign: TextAlign.center,
        obscureText: true,
        keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
        maxLength: 1,
        style: const TextStyle(
          color: AppColors.white,
          fontSize: 24,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
        ),
        decoration: InputDecoration(
          counterText: '',
          filled: true,
          fillColor: AppColors.transparentWhite5,
          enabledBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
            borderSide: BorderSide(
              color: AppColors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.2),
              width: 2,
            ),
          ),
          focusedBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
            borderSide: const BorderSide(
              color: AppColors.accentCyan,
              width: 2,
            ),
          ),
          contentPadding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 12),
        ),
        inputFormatters: [
          FilteringTextInputFormatter.digitsOnly,
          LengthLimitingTextInputFormatter(1),
        ],
        onChanged: (value) => onChanged(index, value),
        onTap: () {
          if (controllers[index].text.isNotEmpty) {
            controllers[index].clear();
            notifyPinChange();
          }
        },
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../core/models/document_category.dart';
import '../../core/models/document_item.dart';
import '../../core/services/document_storage_service.dart';
import '../viewer/document_viewer_screen.dart';

// Sort options enum
enum SortOption {
  name,
  date,
  size,
  type,
}

class CategoryDetailsScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final DocumentCategory category;

  const CategoryDetailsScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.category,
  });

  @override
  State<CategoryDetailsScreen> createState() => _CategoryDetailsScreenState();
}

class _CategoryDetailsScreenState extends State<CategoryDetailsScreen> {
  final DocumentStorageService _storageService = DocumentStorageService();

  List<DocumentItem> documents = [];
  bool isLoading = true;
  int refreshCounter = 0;

  // Sort state variables
  SortOption currentSortOption = SortOption.date; // Default: newest first
  bool isAscending = false; // false = descending (newest/largest first)

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _loadDocuments();
  }

  /// Load documents from storage
  Future<void> _loadDocuments() async {
    if (!mounted) return;

    setState(() => isLoading = true);

    try {
      final docs = await _storageService.getDocumentsByCategory(widget.category.id);
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          documents = docs;
          _applySorting();
          isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() => isLoading = false);
      }
    }
  }

  /// Apply sorting based on current option
  void _applySorting() {
    switch (currentSortOption) {
      case SortOption.name:
        documents.sort((a, b) {
          final comparison = a.name.toLowerCase().compareTo(b.name.toLowerCase());
          return isAscending ? comparison : -comparison;
        });
        break;

      case SortOption.date:
        documents.sort((a, b) {
          final comparison = a.addedAt.compareTo(b.addedAt);
          return isAscending ? comparison : -comparison;
        });
        break;

      case SortOption.size:
        documents.sort((a, b) {
          final comparison = a.fileSize.compareTo(b.fileSize);
          return isAscending ? comparison : -comparison;
        });
        break;

      case SortOption.type:
        documents.sort((a, b) {
          final comparison = a.fileType.compareTo(b.fileType);
          return isAscending ? comparison : -comparison;
        });
        break;
    }
  }

  /// Change sort option
  void _changeSortOption(SortOption newOption) {
    setState(() {
      if (currentSortOption == newOption) {
        // Toggle ascending/descending if same option clicked
        isAscending = !isAscending;
      } else {
        // Change to new option with default order
        currentSortOption = newOption;
        isAscending = newOption == SortOption.name; // Name: A-Z default
      }
      _applySorting();
    });
  }

  /// Open document viewer
  Future<void> _openDocumentViewer(DocumentItem document) async {
    final result = await Navigator.push<bool>(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(
        builder: (context) => DocumentViewerScreen(document: document),
      ),
    );

    if (result == true && mounted) {
      _loadDocuments();
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundLight,
      appBar: AppBar(
        backgroundColor: AppColors.primary,
        foregroundColor: AppColors.white,
        elevation: 0,
        title: Row(
          children: [
            Icon(widget.category.icon, size: 24),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),
            Expanded(
              child: Text(
                widget.category.name,
                style: const TextStyle(
                  fontSize: 20,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        // Sort menu in AppBar
        actions: [
          if (documents.isNotEmpty && !isLoading)
            PopupMenuButton<SortOption>(
              icon: const Icon(Icons.sort, color: Colors.white),
              color: AppColors.primary,
              tooltip: 'Sort documents',
              onSelected: _changeSortOption,
              itemBuilder: (context) => [
                _buildSortMenuItem(
                  SortOption.name,
                  Icons.sort_by_alpha,
                  'Name',
                  'A â†’ Z',
                  'Z â†’ A',
                ),
                _buildSortMenuItem(
                  SortOption.date,
                  Icons.calendar_today,
                  'Date',
                  'Oldest',
                  'Newest',
                ),
                _buildSortMenuItem(
                  SortOption.size,
                  Icons.data_usage,
                  'Size',
                  'Smallest',
                  'Largest',
                ),
                _buildSortMenuItem(
                  SortOption.type,
                  Icons.category,
                  'Type',
                  'PDF â†’ Image',
                  'Image â†’ PDF',
                ),
              ],
            ),
        ],
      ),
      body: SafeArea(
        child: isLoading
            ? const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator(color: AppColors.primary))
            : documents.isEmpty
            ? _buildEmptyState()
            : _buildDocumentsList(),
      ),
    );
  }

  /// Build sort menu item with current selection indicator
  PopupMenuEntry<SortOption> _buildSortMenuItem(
      SortOption option,
      IconData icon,
      String label,
      String ascLabel,
      String descLabel,
      ) {
    final isSelected = currentSortOption == option;
    final orderLabel = isAscending ? ascLabel : descLabel;

    return PopupMenuItem<SortOption>(
      value: option,
      child: Row(
        children: [
          Icon(
            icon,
            color: isSelected ? AppColors.accentCyan : Colors.white,
            size: 20,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          Expanded(
            child: Text(
              label,
              style: TextStyle(
                color: isSelected ? AppColors.accentCyan : Colors.white,
                fontWeight: isSelected ? FontWeight.w700 : FontWeight.w500,
              ),
            ),
          ),
          if (isSelected) ...[
            Text(
              orderLabel,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: AppColors.accentCyan,
                fontSize: 11,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 4),
            Icon(
              isAscending ? Icons.arrow_upward : Icons.arrow_downward,
              color: AppColors.accentCyan,
              size: 16,
            ),
          ],
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  /// Empty state widget
  Widget _buildEmptyState() {
    return Center(
      child: Column(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
        children: [
          Container(
            width: 120,
            height: 120,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.1),
              shape: BoxShape.circle,
            ),
            child: Icon(
              widget.category.icon,
              size: 60,
              color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.3),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 24),
          Text(
            'No ${widget.category.name} Documents',
            style: const TextStyle(
              fontSize: 18,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
              color: AppColors.primary,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          Text(
            'Add your first document from home screen',
            textAlign: TextAlign.center,
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 14,
              color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.6),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  /// Documents list with header + âœ… NEW: Pull-to-Refresh
  Widget _buildDocumentsList() {
    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
      children: [
        // Header with sort info
        Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
          child: Row(
            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
            children: [
              Text(
                '${documents.length} ${documents.length == 1 ? 'Document' : 'Documents'}',
                style: TextStyle(
                  fontSize: 14,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.6),
                ),
              ),
              // Sort indicator chip
              Container(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 10, vertical: 4),
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  color: AppColors.accentCyan.withOpacity(0.1),
                  borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
                  border: Border.all(
                    color: AppColors.accentCyan.withOpacity(0.3),
                    width: 1,
                  ),
                ),
                child: Row(
                  mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
                  children: [
                    Icon(
                      _getSortIcon(),
                      size: 14,
                      color: AppColors.accentCyan,
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 6),
                    Text(
                      _getSortLabel(),
                      style: const TextStyle(
                        fontSize: 11,
                        fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                        color: AppColors.accentCyan,
                      ),
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 4),
                    Icon(
                      isAscending ? Icons.arrow_upward : Icons.arrow_downward,
                      size: 12,
                      color: AppColors.accentCyan,
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
        // âœ… NEW: RefreshIndicator wrapper
        Expanded(
          child: RefreshIndicator(
            color: AppColors.accentCyan,
            backgroundColor: Colors.white,
            onRefresh: _loadDocuments, // Reuse existing load method
            child: ListView.builder(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
              physics: const AlwaysScrollableScrollPhysics(), // âœ… Required for pull-to-refresh
              itemCount: documents.length,
              itemBuilder: (context, index) => _buildDocumentCard(documents[index]),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  /// Get icon for current sort option
  IconData _getSortIcon() {
    switch (currentSortOption) {
      case SortOption.name:
        return Icons.sort_by_alpha;
      case SortOption.date:
        return Icons.calendar_today;
      case SortOption.size:
        return Icons.data_usage;
      case SortOption.type:
        return Icons.category;
    }
  }

  /// Get label for current sort option
  String _getSortLabel() {
    switch (currentSortOption) {
      case SortOption.name:
        return isAscending ? 'A â†’ Z' : 'Z â†’ A';
      case SortOption.date:
        return isAscending ? 'Oldest' : 'Newest';
      case SortOption.size:
        return isAscending ? 'Smallest' : 'Largest';
      case SortOption.type:
        return isAscending ? 'PDF â†’ IMG' : 'IMG â†’ PDF';
    }
  }

  /// Document card widget
  Widget _buildDocumentCard(DocumentItem document) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: () => _openDocumentViewer(document),
      child: Container(
        margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 12),
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: AppColors.white,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          border: Border.all(
            color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.1),
          ),
        ),
        child: Row(
          children: [
            // File icon
            Container(
              width: 48,
              height: 48,
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                color: document.isPdf
                    ? AppColors.error.withOpacity(0.1)
                    : AppColors.accentCyan.withOpacity(0.1),
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
              ),
              child: Icon(
                document.isPdf ? Icons.picture_as_pdf : Icons.description,
                color: document.isPdf ? AppColors.error : AppColors.accentCyan,
                size: 24,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),
            // Document info
            Expanded(
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(
                    document.name,
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 14,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                      color: AppColors.primary,
                    ),
                    maxLines: 1,
                    overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 4),
                  Row(
                    children: [
                      Container(
                        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
                          horizontal: 6,
                          vertical: 2,
                        ),
                        decoration: BoxDecoration(
                          color: document.isPdf
                              ? AppColors.error.withOpacity(0.1)
                              : AppColors.accentCyan.withOpacity(0.1),
                          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(4),
                        ),
                        child: Text(
                          document.fileType.toUpperCase(),
                          style: TextStyle(
                            fontSize: 10,
                            fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                            color: document.isPdf
                                ? AppColors.error
                                : AppColors.accentCyan,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(width: 8),
                      Text(
                        '${document.getFileSizeFormatted()} â€¢ ${document.getTimeAgo()}',
                        style: TextStyle(
                          fontSize: 12,
                          color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.6),
                        ),
                      ),
                    ],
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            ),
            // Chevron icon
            Icon(
              Icons.chevron_right,
              color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.3),
              size: 20,
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../core/services/app_lifecycle_service.dart';
import '../auth/pin_setup_screen.dart';
import 'widgets/dashboard_header.dart';
import 'widgets/stats_card.dart';
import 'widgets/recent_documents.dart';
import 'widgets/categories_grid.dart';
import 'widgets/bottom_navigation.dart';

class DocumentsScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const DocumentsScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<DocumentsScreen> createState() => _DocumentsScreenState();
}

class _DocumentsScreenState extends State<DocumentsScreen> {
  final _lifecycleService = AppLifecycleService();
  int refreshCounter = 0;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _verifyAuthentication();
  }

  /// Verify authentication on screen load
  Future<void> _verifyAuthentication() async {
    final isAuth = await _lifecycleService.isAuthenticated();
    if (!mounted) return;

    if (!isAuth) {
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(
          builder: (_) => const PinSetupScreen(isSetupMode: false),
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  /// âœ… NEW: Refresh all dashboard data
  Future<void> _refreshDashboard() async {
    setState(() {
      refreshCounter++; // Trigger rebuild of child widgets
    });
    // Add small delay for visual feedback
    await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 500));
  }

  /// Refresh documents (called from bottom nav after upload)
  void _refreshDocuments() {
    setState(() {
      refreshCounter++; // Increment to trigger rebuild
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundLight,
      body: SafeArea(
        child: Column(
          children: [
            const DashboardHeader(),
            Expanded(
              // âœ… NEW: RefreshIndicator wrapper
              child: RefreshIndicator(
                color: AppColors.accentCyan,
                backgroundColor: Colors.white,
                onRefresh: _refreshDashboard,
                child: SingleChildScrollView(
                  physics: const AlwaysScrollableScrollPhysics(), // âœ… Required
                  child: Column(
                    children: [
                      const StatsCard(),
                      const SizedBox(height: 16),
                      RecentDocuments(refreshKey: refreshCounter),
                      const SizedBox(height: 24),
                      CategoriesGrid(refreshKey: refreshCounter), // Pass refresh key
                      const SizedBox(height: 120),
                    ],
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      bottomNavigationBar: BottomNavigation(
        onDocumentAdded: _refreshDocuments,
      ),
      extendBody: true,
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
class BottomNavigation extends StatelessWidget {

    super.key,
    this.onDocumentAdded,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.95),
        border: const Border(
          top: BorderSide(
            color: AppColors.primary,
            width: 0.5,

            alignment: Alignment.center,

              Row(
                mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceAround,
                children: [
                  _buildNavItem(Icons.home, 'Home', true, null),
                  _buildNavItem(Icons.folder_open, 'Folders', false, null),
                  const SizedBox(width: 64),
                  _buildNavItem(
                    Icons.search,
                    'Search',
                    false,
                        () => _navigateToSearch(context),
                  ),
                  // âœ… UPDATED: Make Settings functional
                  _buildNavItem(
                    Icons.settings,
                    'Settings',
                    false,
                        () => _navigateToSettings(context),
                  ),
                ],
              ),
              Positioned(
                top: -32,
                child: _buildCentralFAB(context),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  /// Navigate to search screen
  void _navigateToSearch(BuildContext context) {
    Navigator.push(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(
        builder: (context) => const SearchScreen(),
      ),
    );
  }

  /// âœ… NEW: Navigate to settings screen
  void _navigateToSettings(BuildContext context) {
    Navigator.push(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(
        builder: (context) => const SettingsScreen(),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildNavItem(
      IconData icon,
      String label,
      bool isActive,
      VoidCallback? onTap,
      ) {
    return Expanded(
      child: GestureDetector(
        onTap: onTap,
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Icon(
              icon,
              color: isActive
                  ? AppColors.accentCyan
                  : AppColors.primary.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
              size: 24,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 4),
            Text(
              label,
              style: TextStyle(
                fontSize: 11,
                color: isActive
                    ? AppColors.accentCyan
                    : AppColors.primary.withValues(alpha: 0.6),
                fontWeight: isActive ? FontWeight.w600 : FontWeight.w500,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCentralFAB(BuildContext context) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: () => _showUploadOptions(context),
      child: Container(
        width: 64,
        height: 64,
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          gradient: const LinearGradient(
            colors: [AppColors.accentCyan, AppColors.primary],
            begin: Alignment.topLeft,
            end: Alignment.bottomRight,
          ),
          shape: BoxShape.circle,
          boxShadow: [
            BoxShadow(
              color: AppColors.accentCyan.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
              blurRadius: 12,
              offset: const Offset(0, 4),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        child: const Icon(
          Icons.add,
          color: AppColors.white,
          size: 32,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showUploadOptions(BuildContext context) {
    showModalBottomSheet(
      context: context,
      backgroundColor: Colors.transparent,
      isScrollControlled: true,
      builder: (context) => UploadBottomSheet(
        onDocumentAdded: onDocumentAdded,
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/category_data.dart';
import '../../../core/services/document_storage_service.dart';
import '../../../core/models/document_category.dart';
import '../category_details_screen.dart';
import 'category_card.dart';

class CategoriesGrid extends StatefulWidget {
  final int refreshKey; // âœ… NEW: Refresh trigger

  const CategoriesGrid({
    super.key,
    this.refreshKey = 0,
  });

  @override
  State<CategoriesGrid> createState() => _CategoriesGridState();
}

class _CategoriesGridState extends State<CategoriesGrid> {
  final DocumentStorageService _storageService = DocumentStorageService();

  List<DocumentCategory> _categoriesWithCounts = [];
  bool _isLoading = true;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _loadCategoryCounts();
  }

  @override
  void didUpdateWidget(CategoriesGrid oldWidget) {
    super.didUpdateWidget(oldWidget);
    if (oldWidget.refreshKey != widget.refreshKey) {
      _loadCategoryCounts(); // âœ… Reload when refreshKey changes
    }
  }

  Future<void> _loadCategoryCounts() async {
    if (!mounted) return;

    setState(() => _isLoading = true);

    try {
      final List<DocumentCategory> updatedCategories = [];

      for (var category in CategoryData.categories) {
        final count = await _storageService.getCategoryDocumentCount(category.id);
        updatedCategories.add(category.copyWith(documentCount: count));
      }

      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _categoriesWithCounts = updatedCategories;
          _isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() => _isLoading = false);
      }
    }
  }

  void _navigateToCategoryDetails(DocumentCategory category) {
    Navigator.push(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(
        builder: (context) => CategoryDetailsScreen(category: category),
      ),
    ).then((_) {
      // âœ… Refresh counts when coming back
      _loadCategoryCounts();
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          const Text(
            'Categories',
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 16,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              color: AppColors.primary,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 12),
          _isLoading
              ? const Center(
            child: Padding(
              padding: EdgeInsets.all(20),
              child: CircularProgressIndicator(
                color: AppColors.primary,
                strokeWidth: 3,
              ),
            ),
          )
              : GridView.builder(
            shrinkWrap: true,
            physics: const NeverScrollableScrollPhysics(),
            gridDelegate: const SliverGridDelegateWithFixedCrossAxisCount(
              crossAxisCount: 2,
              crossAxisSpacing: 12,
              mainAxisSpacing: 12,
              childAspectRatio: 1.1,
            ),
            itemCount: _categoriesWithCounts.length,
            itemBuilder: (context, index) {
              return CategoryCard(
                category: _categoriesWithCounts[index],
                onTap: () => _navigateToCategoryDetails(_categoriesWithCounts[index]),
              );
            },
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../core/models/document_category.dart';

class CategoryCard extends StatelessWidget {
  final DocumentCategory category;
  final VoidCallback? onTap; // âœ… NEW: Tap callback

  const CategoryCard({
    super.key,
    required this.category,
    this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return InkWell(
      onTap: onTap, // âœ… Execute callback
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(14),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: AppColors.white,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          border: Border.all(
            color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.05),
          ),
          boxShadow: [
            BoxShadow(
              color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.05),
              blurRadius: 4,
              offset: const Offset(0, 2),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        child: Column(
          crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
          children: [
            _buildHeader(),
            const Spacer(),
            _buildTitle(),
            const SizedBox(height: 2),
            _buildSubtitle(),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildHeader() {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
      children: [
        Container(
          width: 40,
          height: 40,
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.05),
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
          ),
          child: Icon(
            category.icon,
            color: AppColors.primary,
            size: 20,
          ),
        ),
        Container(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
            horizontal: 8,
            vertical: 4,
          ),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.1),
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          ),
          child: Text(
            '${category.documentCount}', // âœ… Shows actual count
            style: const TextStyle(
              fontSize: 10,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              color: AppColors.primary,
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildTitle() {
    return Text(
      category.name,
      style: const TextStyle(
        fontSize: 14,
        fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
        color: AppColors.primary,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildSubtitle() {
    return Text(
      category.subtitle,
      style: TextStyle(
        fontSize: 10,
        fontWeight: FontWeight.w500,
        color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.5),
      ),
    );
  }
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';

class DashboardHeader extends StatelessWidget {
  const DashboardHeader({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
        children: [
          const Text(
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../core/services/document_storage_service.dart';
import '../../../core/models/document_item.dart';
import '../../viewer/document_viewer_screen.dart';

class RecentDocuments extends StatefulWidget {
  final int refreshKey;

  const RecentDocuments({
    super.key,
    this.refreshKey = 0,
  });

  @override
  State<RecentDocuments> createState() => _RecentDocumentsState();
}

class _RecentDocumentsState extends State<RecentDocuments> {
  final DocumentStorageService _storageService = DocumentStorageService();

  List<DocumentItem> documents = [];
  bool isLoading = true;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _loadDocuments();
  }

  @override
  void didUpdateWidget(RecentDocuments oldWidget) {
    super.didUpdateWidget(oldWidget);
    if (oldWidget.refreshKey != widget.refreshKey) {
      _loadDocuments();
    }
  }

  /// Load documents from storage
  Future<void> _loadDocuments() async {
    if (!mounted) return;

    setState(() => isLoading = true);

    try {
      final docs = await _storageService.getRecentDocuments(limit: 5);
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          documents = docs;
          isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() => isLoading = false);
      }
    }
  }

  /// Open document viewer
  Future<void> _openDocumentViewer(DocumentItem document) async {
    final result = await Navigator.push<bool>(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(
        builder: (context) => DocumentViewerScreen(document: document),
      ),
    );

    if (result == true && mounted) {
      _loadDocuments();
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          const Text(
            'Recent Documents',
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 16,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              color: AppColors.primary,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 12),
          if (isLoading)
            const Center(
              child: Padding(
                padding: EdgeInsets.all(20),
                child: CircularProgressIndicator(color: AppColors.primary),
              ),
            )
          else if (documents.isEmpty)
            _buildEmptyState()
          else
          // âœ… NEW: Wrap with RefreshIndicator
            SizedBox(
              height: documents.length * 80.0, // Approximate height per item
              child: RefreshIndicator(
                color: AppColors.accentCyan,
                backgroundColor: Colors.white,
                onRefresh: _loadDocuments,
                child: ListView.builder(
                  physics: const AlwaysScrollableScrollPhysics(), // âœ… Required
                  itemCount: documents.length,
                  itemBuilder: (context, index) => _buildDocumentCard(documents[index]),
                ),
              ),
            ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  /// Empty state widget
  Widget _buildEmptyState() {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        border: Border.all(
          color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.1),
        ),
      ),
      child: const Center(
        child: Text(
          'No documents yet. Add your first document!',
          textAlign: TextAlign.center,
          style: TextStyle(
            color: AppColors.textSecondary,
            fontSize: 14,
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  /// Document card widget
  Widget _buildDocumentCard(DocumentItem document) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: () => _openDocumentViewer(document),
      child: Container(
        margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 12),
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: AppColors.white,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          border: Border.all(
            color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.1),
          ),
        ),
        child: Row(
          children: [
            // File icon
            Container(
              width: 48,
              height: 48,
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                color: document.isPdf
                    ? AppColors.error.withOpacity(0.1)
                    : AppColors.accentCyan.withOpacity(0.1),
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
              ),
              child: Icon(
                document.isPdf ? Icons.picture_as_pdf : Icons.description,
                color: document.isPdf ? AppColors.error : AppColors.accentCyan,
                size: 24,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),
            // Document info
            Expanded(
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(
                    document.name,
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 14,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                      color: AppColors.primary,
                    ),
                    maxLines: 1,
                    overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 4),
                  Row(
                    children: [
                      Container(
                        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
                          horizontal: 6,
                          vertical: 2,
                        ),
                        decoration: BoxDecoration(
                          color: document.isPdf
                              ? AppColors.error.withOpacity(0.1)
                              : AppColors.accentCyan.withOpacity(0.1),
                          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(4),
                        ),
                        child: Text(
                          document.fileType.toUpperCase(),
                          style: TextStyle(
                            fontSize: 10,
                            fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                            color: document.isPdf
                                ? AppColors.error
                                : AppColors.accentCyan,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(width: 8),
                      Text(
                        '${document.getFileSizeFormatted()} â€¢ ${document.getTimeAgo()}',
                        style: TextStyle(
                          fontSize: 12,
                          color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.6),
                        ),
                      ),
                    ],
                  ),
                ],
              ),

            // Chevron icon
            Icon(
              Icons.chevron_right,
              color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.3),
              size: 20,
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../core/services/document_storage_service.dart';

class StatsCard extends StatefulWidget {
  const StatsCard({super.key});

  @override
  State<StatsCard> createState() => _StatsCardState();
}

class _StatsCardState extends State<StatsCard> {
  final DocumentStorageService _storageService = DocumentStorageService();
  int _documentCount = 0;
  int _storageUsed = 0;
  bool _isLoading = true;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _loadStats();
  }

  Future<void> _loadStats() async {
    final count = await _storageService.getDocumentCount();
    final storage = await _storageService.getTotalStorageUsed();

    if (mounted) {
      setState(() {
        _documentCount = count;
        _storageUsed = storage;
        _isLoading = false;
      });
    }
  }

  String _formatBytes(int bytes) {
    if (bytes < 1024) {
      return '$bytes B';
    } else if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) {
      return '${(bytes / 1024).toStringAsFixed(1)} KB';
    } else {
      return '${(bytes / (1024 * 1024)).toStringAsFixed(1)} MB';
    }
  }

  double _getStoragePercentage() {
    const int maxStorage = 5 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024; // 5 GB
    return _storageUsed / maxStorage;
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
        border: Border.all(
          color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.05),
        ),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.08),
            blurRadius: 8,
            offset: const Offset(0, 2),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: Column(
        children: [
          _buildHeader(),
          const SizedBox(height: 20),
          _buildStorageInfo(),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildHeader() {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
      children: [
        Column(
          crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
          children: [
            Text(
              'Total Vault Documents',
              style: TextStyle(
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w500,
                color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.6),
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 4),
            _isLoading
                ? const SizedBox(
              width: 40,
              height: 40,
              child: CircularProgressIndicator(
                strokeWidth: 3,
                color: AppColors.primary,
              ),
            )
                : Text(
              '$_documentCount',
              style: const TextStyle(
                fontSize: 36,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w800,
                color: AppColors.primary,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        Container(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
            horizontal: 12,
            vertical: 6,
          ),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: AppColors.accentCyan.withOpacity(0.1),
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
          ),
          child: const Text(
            'SECURE',
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 10,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              color: AppColors.accentCyan,
              letterSpacing: 1.2,
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildStorageInfo() {
    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
      children: [
        Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
          children: [
            Text(
              'STORAGE USED',
              style: TextStyle(
                fontSize: 10,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.6),
                letterSpacing: 1.2,
              ),
            ),
            Text(
              '${_formatBytes(_storageUsed)} / 5 GB',
              style: const TextStyle(
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                color: AppColors.primary,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 8),
        _buildProgressBar(),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildProgressBar() {
    return Container(
      height: 8,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.1),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(4),
      ),
      child: FractionallySizedBox(
        alignment: Alignment.centerLeft,
        widthFactor: _getStoragePercentage(),
        child: Container(
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: AppColors.accentCyan,
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(4),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 64: upload_bottom_sheet.dart

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/upload_options_data.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/category_data.dart'; // âœ… NEW
import '../../../core/models/upload_option.dart';
import '../../../core/models/document_category.dart'; // âœ… NEW
import '../../../core/services/camera_service.dart';
import '../../../core/services/gallery_service.dart';
import '../../../core/services/pdf_picker_service.dart';
import '../../../core/services/document_storage_service.dart';
import 'upload_sheet_header.dart';
import 'upload_option_card.dart';

class UploadBottomSheet extends StatefulWidget {
  final Function? onDocumentAdded;

  const UploadBottomSheet({
    super.key,
    this.onDocumentAdded,
  });

  @override
  State<UploadBottomSheet> createState() => _UploadBottomSheetState();
}

class _UploadBottomSheetState extends State<UploadBottomSheet> {
  final CameraService _cameraService = CameraService();
  final GalleryService _galleryService = GalleryService();
  final PdfPickerService _pdfPickerService = PdfPickerService();
  final DocumentStorageService _storageService = DocumentStorageService();

  bool _isProcessing = false;
  String _selectedCategoryId = 'other'; // âœ… NEW: Default category

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: const BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.vertical(top: Radius.circular(24)),
      ),
      child: Column(
        mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
        children: [
          const UploadSheetHeader(),
          const SizedBox(height: 20),

          // âœ… NEW: Category Selector
          _buildCategorySelector(),
          const SizedBox(height: 20),

          if (_isProcessing)
            const Padding(
              padding: EdgeInsets.all(40),
              child: CircularProgressIndicator(color: AppColors.primary),
            )
          else
            ...UploadOptionsData.options.map((option) => Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 12),
              child: UploadOptionCard(
                option: option,
                onTap: () => _handleOptionTap(option),
              ),
            )),
          const SizedBox(height: 20),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  // âœ… NEW: Category Dropdown Widget
  Widget _buildCategorySelector() {
    final selectedCategory = CategoryData.categories
        .firstWhere((cat) => cat.id == _selectedCategoryId);

    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 12),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.05),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        border: Border.all(
          color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.1),
        ),
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          Icon(
            selectedCategory.icon,
            color: AppColors.primary,
            size: 20,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          Expanded(
            child: DropdownButtonHideUnderline(
              child: DropdownButton<String>(
                value: _selectedCategoryId,
                isExpanded: true,
                icon: const Icon(Icons.arrow_drop_down, color: AppColors.primary),
                style: const TextStyle(
                  fontSize: 14,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  color: AppColors.primary,
                ),
                items: CategoryData.categories.map((category) {
                  return DropdownMenuItem<String>(
                    value: category.id,
                    child: Row(
                      children: [
                        Icon(category.icon, size: 18, color: AppColors.primary),
                        const SizedBox(width: 8),
                        Text(category.name),
                      ],
                    ),
                  );
                }).toList(),
                onChanged: (String? newValue) {
                  if (newValue != null) {
                    setState(() {
                      _selectedCategoryId = newValue;
                    });
                  }
                },
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  void _handleOptionTap(UploadOption option) {
    switch (option.type) {
      case UploadType.camera:
        _handleCameraScan();
        break;
      case UploadType.gallery:
        _handleGalleryPick();
        break;
      case UploadType.pdf:
        _handlePdfPick();
        break;
    }
  }

  Future<void> _handleCameraScan() async {
    setState(() => _isProcessing = true);

    try {
      final result = await _cameraService.captureFromCamera();

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (!result.success) {
        _showError(result.error ?? 'Failed to capture photo');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      if (result.imageFile == null) {
        _showError('No image captured');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      final String? documentName = await _showNameInputDialog();

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (documentName == null || documentName.trim().isEmpty) {
        await result.imageFile!.delete();
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      final saveResult = await _storageService.saveDocument(
        imageFile: result.imageFile!,
        documentName: documentName.trim(),
        categoryId: _selectedCategoryId, // âœ… Use selected category
      );

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (!saveResult.success) {
        _showError(saveResult.error ?? 'Failed to save document');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      _showSuccess('Document saved successfully!');
      widget.onDocumentAdded?.call();

      await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 1500));
      if (mounted) Navigator.pop(context);
    } catch (e) {
      if (mounted) {
        _showError('Unexpected error: ${e.toString()}');
      }
    } finally {
      if (mounted) setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
    }
  }

  Future<void> _handleGalleryPick() async {
    setState(() => _isProcessing = true);

    try {
      final result = await _galleryService.pickFromGallery();

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (!result.success) {
        _showError(result.error ?? 'Failed to pick image');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      if (result.imageFile == null) {
        _showError('No image selected');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      final String? documentName = await _showNameInputDialog();

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (documentName == null || documentName.trim().isEmpty) {
        await result.imageFile!.delete();
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      final saveResult = await _storageService.saveDocument(
        imageFile: result.imageFile!,
        documentName: documentName.trim(),
        categoryId: _selectedCategoryId, // âœ… Use selected category
      );

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (!saveResult.success) {
        _showError(saveResult.error ?? 'Failed to save document');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      _showSuccess('Document saved successfully!');
      widget.onDocumentAdded?.call();

      await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 1500));
      if (mounted) Navigator.pop(context);
    } catch (e) {
      if (mounted) {
        _showError('Unexpected error: ${e.toString()}');
      }
    } finally {
      if (mounted) setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
    }
  }

  Future<void> _handlePdfPick() async {
    setState(() => _isProcessing = true);

    try {
      final result = await _pdfPickerService.pickPdf();

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (!result.success) {
        _showError(result.error ?? 'Failed to pick PDF');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      if (result.pdfFile == null) {
        _showError('No PDF selected');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      final String? documentName = await _showNameInputDialog(
        suggestedName: result.fileName?.replaceAll('.pdf', '') ?? '',
      );

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (documentName == null || documentName.trim().isEmpty) {
        await result.pdfFile!.delete();
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      final saveResult = await _storageService.saveDocument(
        imageFile: result.pdfFile!,
        documentName: documentName.trim(),
        categoryId: _selectedCategoryId, // âœ… Use selected category
      );

      if (!mounted) return;

      if (!saveResult.success) {
        _showError(saveResult.error ?? 'Failed to save PDF');
        setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
        return;
      }

      _showSuccess('PDF saved successfully!');
      widget.onDocumentAdded?.call();

      await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 1500));
      if (mounted) Navigator.pop(context);
    } catch (e) {
      if (mounted) {
        _showError('Unexpected error: ${e.toString()}');
      }
    } finally {
      if (mounted) setState(() => _isProcessing = false);
    }
  }

  Future<String?> _showNameInputDialog({String? suggestedName}) async {
    final TextEditingController controller = TextEditingController(
      text: suggestedName ?? '',
    );

    return showDialog<String>(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        backgroundColor: AppColors.white,
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16)),
        title: const Text(
          'Document Name',
          style: TextStyle(
            color: AppColors.primary,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
          ),
        ),
        content: TextField(
          controller: controller,
          autofocus: true,
          decoration: InputDecoration(
            hintText: 'Enter document name',
            filled: true,
            fillColor: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.05),
            border: OutlineInputBorder(
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
              borderSide: BorderSide.none,
            ),
          ),
        ),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
            child: const Text('Cancel'),
          ),
          ElevatedButton(
            style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
              backgroundColor: AppColors.primary,
              foregroundColor: AppColors.white,
            ),
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, controller.text),
            child: const Text('Save'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showError(String message) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text(message),
        backgroundColor: AppColors.error,
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showSuccess(String message) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text(message),
        backgroundColor: AppColors.success,
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../core/models/upload_option.dart';

class UploadOptionCard extends StatelessWidget {
  final UploadOption option;
  final VoidCallback onTap;

  const UploadOptionCard({
    super.key,
    required this.option,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Material(
      color: Colors.transparent,
      child: InkWell(
        onTap: onTap,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        child: Container(
          height: 68,
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: AppColors.backgroundLight,
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
            border: Border.all(
              color: AppColors.gray200,
              width: 1,
            ),
          ),
          child: Row(
            children: [
              _buildIconContainer(),
              const SizedBox(width: 16),
              _buildTitle(),
              const Spacer(),
              _buildChevron(),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildIconContainer() {
    return Container(
      width: 48,
      height: 48,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: option.color.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
      ),
      child: Icon(
        option.icon,
        color: option.color,
        size: 24,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildTitle() {
    return Text(
      option.title,
      style: const TextStyle(
        fontSize: 16,
        fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
        color: AppColors.primary,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildChevron() {
    return Icon(
      Icons.chevron_right,
      color: AppColors.gray400,
      size: 24,
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../core/services/app_lifecycle_service.dart';
import '../auth/pin_setup_screen.dart';

class HomeScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const HomeScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<HomeScreen> createState() => _HomeScreenState();
}

class _HomeScreenState extends State<HomeScreen> {
  final _lifecycleService = AppLifecycleService();

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _verifyAuthentication();
  }

  /// âœ… Double-check authentication on screen load
  /// Redirects to PIN screen if user is not authenticated
  /// Prevents unauthorized access to Home screen
  Future<void> _verifyAuthentication() async {
    final isAuth = await _lifecycleService.isAuthenticated();

    // âœ… Check mounted BEFORE using context
    if (!mounted) return;

    if (!isAuth) {
      // Redirect to PIN screen if not authenticated
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(
          builder: (_) => const PinSetupScreen(isSetupMode: false),
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  /// âœ… Handles logout with proper async context management
  Future<void> _handleLogout() async {
    // Show dialog and get result
    final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
      context: context,
      builder: (dialogContext) => AlertDialog(
        backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundDark,
        title: const Text(
          'Logout',
          style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.white),
        ),
        content: const Text(
          'Are you sure you want to logout?',
          style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.white),
        ),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(dialogContext, false),
            child: const Text('Cancel'),
          ),
          ElevatedButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(dialogContext, true),
            style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
              backgroundColor: Colors.red,
            ),
            child: const Text('Logout'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );

    // âœ… Check mounted after async dialog
    if (!mounted) return;

    // If user confirmed logout
    if (confirm == true) {
      // âœ… FIXED: Changed lockApp() to logout() (Line 79)
      await _lifecycleService.logout();

      // âœ… Check mounted again after async logout
      if (!mounted) return;

      // Navigate to PIN screen
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(
          builder: (_) => const PinSetupScreen(isSetupMode: false),
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundDark,
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: const Text('My Vault'),
        backgroundColor: AppColors.primary,
        actions: [
          IconButton(
            icon: const Icon(Icons.logout),
            onPressed: _handleLogout,
            tooltip: 'Logout',
          ),
        ],
      ),
      body: Center(
        child: Column(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: [
            const Icon(
              Icons.check_circle,
              color: AppColors.accentCyan,
              size: 80,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 24),
            const Text(
              'Welcome to ID Locker!',
              style: TextStyle(
                color: AppColors.white,
                fontSize: 24,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 12),
            Text(
              'Your vault is secured',
              style: TextStyle(
                color: AppColors.white.withValues(alpha: 0.6),
                fontSize: 16,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 32),
            ElevatedButton.icon(
              onPressed: () {
                // TODO: Navigate to documents
              },
              icon: const Icon(Icons.folder),
              label: const Text('My Documents'),
              style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
                backgroundColor: AppColors.accentCyan,
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
                  horizontal: 32,
                  vertical: 16,
                ),
              ),
            ),
```

### File 68: onboarding_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\onboarding\onboarding_screen.dart`
**Size:** 3.25 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../core/constants/onboarding_data.dart';
import '../../core/services/app_initialization_service.dart';
import 'widgets/onboarding_slide.dart';
import 'widgets/page_indicator.dart';
import 'widgets/next_button.dart';

class OnboardingScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const OnboardingScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<OnboardingScreen> createState() => _OnboardingScreenState();
}

class _OnboardingScreenState extends State<OnboardingScreen> {
  final PageController _pageController = PageController();
  final AppInitializationService _initService = AppInitializationService();

  int _currentPage = 0;
  bool _isNavigating = false;

  void _onPageChanged(int page) {
    setState(() {
      _currentPage = page;
    });
  }

  Future<void> _nextPage() async {
    if (_isNavigating) return;

    final isLastPage = _currentPage == OnboardingData.items.length - 1;

    if (isLastPage) {
      setState(() => _isNavigating = true);

      await _initService.setOnboardingCompleted();

      if (!mounted) return;

      Navigator.pushNamedAndRemoveUntil(
        context,
        '/createpin',
            (route) => false,
      );
    } else {
      _pageController.nextPage(
        duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 350),
        curve: Curves.easeInOut,
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _pageController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final isLastPage = _currentPage == OnboardingData.items.length - 1;

    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundLight,
      body: SafeArea(
        child: Column(
          children: [
            Expanded(
              child: PageView.builder(
                controller: _pageController,
                onPageChanged: _onPageChanged,
                itemCount: OnboardingData.items.length,
                itemBuilder: (context, index) {
                  return OnboardingSlide(
                    item: OnboardingData.items[index],
                  );
                },
              ),
            ),

            Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 40),
              child: PageIndicator(
                currentPage: _currentPage,
                pageCount: OnboardingData.items.length,
              ),
            ),

            Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(32, 0, 32, 48),
              child: Row(
                mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                children: [
                  const SizedBox(width: 48),
                  Expanded(
                    child: Center(
                      child: NextButton(
                        text: isLastPage ? 'Get Started' : 'Next',
                        onPressed: _isNavigating ? null : () => _nextPage(),  // âœ… FIXED: Wrap async in sync callback
                        isLastPage: isLastPage,
                      ),
                    ),
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(width: 48),
                ],
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class NextButton extends StatelessWidget {

    super.key,
    required this.text,
    required this.onPressed,
    this.isLastPage = false,

              fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/onboarding_data.dart';

class OnboardingSlide extends StatelessWidget {
  final OnboardingItem item;

  const OnboardingSlide({
    super.key,
    required this.item,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return SingleChildScrollView(
      child: Padding(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 32),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: [
            const SizedBox(height: 40),
            _buildIllustration(),
            const SizedBox(height: 48),
            _buildTitle(),
            const SizedBox(height: 16),
            _buildDescription(),
            const SizedBox(height: 40),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildIllustration() {
    return Container(
      width: double.infinity,
      height: 320,
      constraints: const BoxConstraints(maxWidth: 320),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: const Color(0xFFF6F7F9),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
      ),
      child: Stack(
        children: [
          _buildDecorativeBlurs(),
          _buildMainCard(),
          _buildFloatingDocument(),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildDecorativeBlurs() {
    return Stack(
      children: [
        Positioned(
          top: -40,
          left: -40,
          child: Container(
            width: 160,
            height: 160,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              shape: BoxShape.circle,
              color: item.accentColor.withValues(alpha: 0.08),
            ),
          ),
        ),
        Positioned(
          bottom: -20,
          right: -20,
          child: Container(
            width: 130,
            height: 130,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              shape: BoxShape.circle,
              color: AppColors.primary.withValues(alpha: 0.05),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildMainCard() {
    return Center(
      child: Container(
        width: 192,
        height: 256,
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: AppColors.white,
          border: Border.all(
            color: AppColors.primary,
            width: 4,
          ),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
          boxShadow: [
            BoxShadow(
              color: item.accentColor.withValues(alpha: 0.25),
              blurRadius: 32,
              offset: const Offset(0, 8),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        child: Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
          child: Column(
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
            children: [
              _buildCardLine(0.65, item.accentColor.withValues(alpha: 0.25)),
              const SizedBox(height: 12),
              _buildCardLine(1.0, AppColors.gray200),
              const SizedBox(height: 8),
              _buildCardLine(1.0, AppColors.gray200),
              const SizedBox(height: 8),
              _buildCardLine(0.5, AppColors.gray200),
              const Spacer(),
              Center(
                child: Container(
                  width: 64,
                  height: 64,
                  decoration: BoxDecoration(
                    shape: BoxShape.circle,
                    color: item.accentColor,
                    boxShadow: [
                      BoxShadow(
                        color: item.accentColor.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
                        blurRadius: 16,
                        offset: const Offset(0, 4),
                      ),
                    ],
                  ),
                  child: Icon(
                    item.primaryIcon,
                    color: AppColors.white,
                    size: 30,
                  ),
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(height: 12),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCardLine(double widthFactor, Color color) {
    return Container(
      width: 160 * widthFactor,
      height: 12,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: color,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(6),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFloatingDocument() {
    return Positioned(
      right: 16,
      top: 80,
      child: Transform.rotate(
        angle: 0.2,
        child: Container(
          width: 80,
          height: 96,
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: item.accentColor.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
            border: Border.all(
              color: item.accentColor.withValues(alpha: 0.2),
              width: 1,
            ),
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          ),
          child: Icon(
            item.secondaryIcon,
            color: item.accentColor,
            size: 48,
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  // âœ… FIXED: Text ab clearly visible hoga
  Widget _buildTitle() {
    return Text(
      item.title,
      textAlign: TextAlign.center,
      style: const TextStyle(
        color: Color(0xFF2b3d4f), // âœ… Direct dark color for visibility
        fontSize: 32,
        fontWeight: FontWeight.w800,
        height: 1.1,
        letterSpacing: -0.5,
      ),
    );
  }

  // âœ… FIXED: Description text ab visible hoga
  Widget _buildDescription() {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
      child: Text(
        item.description,
        textAlign: TextAlign.center,
        style: const TextStyle(
          color: Color(0xFF5a6c7d), // âœ… Medium gray for readability
          fontSize: 17,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.w500,
          height: 1.5,
        ),
      ),
    );
```

### File 71: page_indicator.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\onboarding\widgets\page_indicator.dart`
**Size:** 1.01 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';

class PageIndicator extends StatelessWidget {
  final int currentPage;
  final int pageCount;

  const PageIndicator({
    super.key,
    required this.currentPage,
    required this.pageCount,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
      children: List.generate(
        pageCount,
            (index) => _buildDot(index == currentPage, index),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildDot(bool isActive, int index) {
    return AnimatedContainer(
      duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 300),
      margin: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 5),
      width: isActive ? 24 : 10,
      height: 10,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: isActive
            ? AppColors.accentCyan
            : AppColors.primary.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(5),
      ),
    );
  }
}

```
